## Decree-Law No. 61 of 2025
### Extending the period stipulated in Law No. 3 of 2016 authorizing the Government to take an amount from the General Reserve Fund <orig>المال الاحتياطي العام</orig>

- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And the Amiri Order <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH, corresponding to May 10, 2024 AD,
- And Law No. 24 of 1963 establishing the Supreme Defense Council <orig>مجلس الدفاع الأعلى</orig>, as amended by Decree-Law No. 53 of 1987,
- And Decree-Law No. 31 of 1978 regarding the rules for preparing general budgets, supervising their implementation, and the final account, and its amending laws,
- And Decree-Law No. 27 of 1981 increasing the amounts allocated for strengthening the country's defense, as amended by Decree-Law No. 33 of 1987,
- And Decree-Law No. 35 of 1988 increasing the amounts allocated for strengthening the country's defense,
- And Decree-Law No. 46 of 1992 increasing the amounts allocated for strengthening the country's defense, and its amending laws,
- And Law No. 3 of 2016 authorizing the Government to take an amount from the General Reserve Fund <orig>المال الاحتياطي العام</orig>,
- And Decree No. 84 of 2024 concerning ministerial substitutions and delegations, and its amending decrees,
- And upon the proposal of the Minister of Defense <orig>وزير الدفاع</orig>,
- And with the approval of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>,
- We have issued the following Decree-Law:

### Article One
The period stipulated in Articles One and Two of the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016 is extended for two additional fiscal years.
<page_end>1</page_end>

### Article Two
The Prime Minister and the Ministers – each within their respective jurisdictions – shall implement this Decree-Law, and it shall come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette.

**Amir of Kuwait**
**Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah**

**Acting Prime Minister**
**Fahad Yousef Saud Al-Sabah**

**Minister of Defense**
**Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Salem Al-Sabah**

Issued at Seif Palace on: 27 Ramadan 1446 H
Corresponding to: 27 March 2025 AD

# Explanatory Memorandum
## To Decree-Law No. 61 of 2025
### Extending the Period Stipulated in Law No. 3 of 2016
Authorizing the Government to Take an Amount of Money from the General Reserve

Law No. 3 of 2016 was issued authorizing the government to take a specified amount of money from the General Reserve <orig>الاحتياطي العام</orig> to enhance the state's defense capabilities over a period of ten fiscal years, starting from the 2015/2016 fiscal year, in order to keep pace with regional developments and ensure the readiness of the Armed Forces.

Given the approaching end of the time period specified by the aforementioned law, and the continuing need to complete the approved defense projects, it has become necessary to extend this period for an additional two fiscal years.

This extension aims to enable the competent authorities to complete the armament and military equipment programs according to pre-established plans, without exceeding the amount specified in the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016. No amendment has been made to the allocated expenditure amount; the extension is limited to granting more time to complete the existing defense projects.

The Supreme Defense Council <orig>مجلس الدفاع الأعلى</orig> shall continue to exercise its powers as specified under the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016, including supervising the allocation and disbursement of the approved amounts, and overseeing the implementation of contracts to ensure the optimal use of financial resources and the achievement of the established defense objectives.

And whereas the Amiri Order <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> was issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 H, corresponding to 10/5/2024 AD, stipulating in its Article (4) that laws shall be issued by decree-laws, the accompanying draft Decree-Law, consisting of two articles, has been prepared.

The first article of the draft provides for the extension of the period stipulated in the first and second articles of the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016 for an additional two fiscal years. The second article of the draft obligates the Prime Minister and the Ministers to implement it and for it to come into force from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.
<page_end>2</page_end>

# Decree No. 61 of 2025
## Amending Decree No. 139 of 2024
## Concerning Judicial Promotions and Transfers

- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And the Amiri Order issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 H, corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
- And Decree-Law No. 14 of 1977 concerning the grades and salaries of judges, members of the Public Prosecution, and the Fatwa and Legislation Department, and its amending laws,
- And the Law on the Organization of the Judiciary, issued by Decree-Law No. 23 of 1990, and its amending laws,
- And Decree No. 57 of 1990 concerning the salaries and allowances of judges, members of the Public Prosecution, and the Fatwa and Legislation Department, and its amending decrees,
- And Decree No. 108 of 2003 concerning the salaries and allowances of judges and members of the Public Prosecution, as amended by Decree No. 23 of 2004,
- And Decree No. 41 of 2009 regarding the granting of a special judicial allowance to judges and members of the Public Prosecution, and its amendments by Decree No. 162 of 2011 and Decree No. 126 of 2018,
- And Decree No. 84 of 2024 concerning ministerial substitutions and delegations, and its amending decrees,
- And Decree No. 139 of 2024 concerning judicial promotions and transfers,
- And upon the approval of the Supreme Judicial Council <orig>المجلس الأعلى للقضاء</orig> in its session No. (29/2024) held on 17/9/2024,
- And based on the proposal of the Minister of Justice <orig>وزير العدل</orig>,
- And with the approval of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>,

**We have decreed the following**

The order of the names listed in Article One of Decree No. 139 of 2024 concerning judicial promotions and transfers shall be amended to read as follows:

### Article Two
The Minister of Justice shall implement this decree, and it shall be published in the Official Gazette.

**Acting Prime Minister**

  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains two decisions from the Capital Markets Authority: Decision No. 53/2025 renewing the license for the Boubyan Multi-Asset Holding Fund, and Decision No. 54/2025 amending regulations to exclude certain insurance products from collective investment schemes."

<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1733 Seventy-First Year

5

Has decided the following

**Article One**
To renew the license of the collective investment scheme for the Boubyan Multi-Asset Holding Fund, for a renewable period of three years, effective from 2025/04/25.

**Article Two**
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall come into effect from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Head of the Supervision Sector
Ziad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>

Issued on: April 2, 2025 AD

# Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
## Decision No. (54) of 2025
### Regarding the Exemption of Insurance Products from Collective Investment Schemes

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority and the Regulation of Securities Activities, and its Executive Bylaws and their amendments.
- And the decision of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> No. (CMA/BOC 8-9 of 2025) issued in its meeting No. (9) of 2025 held on 2025/03/26.

Has decided the following:

**Article One:**
Article (1-1-2) of Book Thirteen (Collective Investment Schemes) of the Executive Bylaws of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority and the Regulation of Securities Activities and its amendments shall be amended as shown in Attachment No. (1) to this decision.

**Article Two:**
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall come into effect from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Acting Executive Director
Othman Ibrahim Al-Issa <orig>عثمان إبراهيم العيسى</orig>

Issued on: April 2, 2025 AD

<table_caption>Attachment No. (1): Amendments to Collective Investment Scheme Regulations</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Book | Chapter | Article | Type of Amendment | Text Before Amendment | Text After Amendment |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Thirteen | One | 1-1-2 | Article Amendment | The following are not included within collective investment schemes: 1. Insurance contracts and their associated investment instruments, and investments managed as part of Takaful insurance contracts. 2. Investment accounts with Islamic banks subject to the supervision of the Central Bank. 3. Investment portfolios. 4. Contracts made between companies belonging to the same group. 5. Savings, pension, retirement, or benefit schemes established for the benefit of company employees. 6. Any other cases that the Authority decides to exclude from the scope of collective investment schemes. | The following are not included within collective investment schemes: 1. Insurance products whose purpose is the payment of specific amounts due to death, disability, reaching a certain age, or upon the expiry of the agreed term, or life insurance where the client does not bear the investment results, whether profit or loss. 2. Investment accounts with Islamic banks subject to the supervision of the Central Bank. 3. Investment portfolios. 4. Contracts made between companies belonging to the same group. 5. Savings, pension, retirement, or benefit schemes established for the benefit of company employees. 6. Any other cases that the Authority decides to exclude from the scope of collective investment schemes. |
</table>

| 1 | Two | 1-2-6 | Article Amendment | A committee for receiving complaints and grievances shall be formed by a resolution of the Board, consisting of no more than four members with expertise in financial, economic, and legal affairs, including a chairman and a deputy chairman of the committee, for a term of two years, renewable once. <page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Decision No. (56) of 2025 regarding a special marketing license for Kuwait Financial Centre",
  "document_date": "2025-04-06",
  "issue_number": 1733,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "decree",
  "languages_detected": ["ar", "en"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Ziad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>",
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains Decision No. (56) of 2025, which grants a license to Kuwait Financial Centre to market 35,000 shares of MKZ Development 46 within Kuwait, specifying the terms and conditions of the offering."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
8
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 H – 6/4/2025 G
</header>


Has decided the following
## First Article
Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig> is licensed to market 35,000 shares (only thirty-five thousand shares) of MKZ Development 46, established in the Cayman Islands, through a private placement within the State of Kuwait, with an offer price of 1,000 Euros (only one thousand Euros) per share.

## Second Article
The shares to be marketed within the State of Kuwait shall be offered to Professional Clients only, as stipulated in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Bylaws of Law No. 7 of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, and their amendments. The entity receiving subscription applications shall be:
* Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig>.

## Third Article
The objectives of the Collective Investment Scheme shall be determined based on the information provided in the Prospectus.

## Fourth Article
The term of the marketing license is one year, renewable annually, commencing from the date of issuance of the Authority's license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.

## Fifth Article
The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this decision. In the event of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, this decision shall be considered null and void.

## Sixth Article
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Head of the Supervision Sector
Ziad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>

Issued on: 02 April 2025 G
<page_end>8</page_end>

M.H. 9-9 for the year 2025 and M.M.H. 11-9 for the year 2025) in its meeting No. (9) for the year 2025, held on 26/03/2025,

Has decided the following:

### Article One:
Appendix No. (4) concerning the schedule of fees for the Authority's services from Book Two (Capital Markets Authority) of the Executive Bylaws of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and their amendments shall be amended in accordance with Appendix No. (1) of this decision.

Book Five (Securities Activities and Registered Persons) of the Executive Bylaws of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and their amendments shall be amended in accordance with Appendix No. (3) of this decision.

### Article Four:
Each of Appendix No. (7) "Application Form for Cancellation of Securities Activities," and (11) "Application Form for Approval of Actual Control over a Licensed Person" from Book Five (Securities Activities and Registered Persons) regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and their amendments shall be amended in accordance with Appendix No. (4) of this decision.

### Article Five:
The competent authorities shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall come into effect from the date of its issuance and shall be published in the Official Gazette.

Acting Executive Director
Othman Ibrahim Al-Issa <orig>عثمان إبراهيم العيسى</orig>

| 15-1-1 | Request to cancel the license for securities activities. | 1,000 K.D. (One Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ألف دينار كويتي</orig>) | Upon submission of the cancellation request. |
| 16-1-1 | Resumption of a restricted or suspended activity. | 1,000 K.D. (One Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ألف دينار كويتي</orig>) | After the Authority's approval. |
</table>

|---|---|---|---|

# 11: Withdrawal of a Service Application (Refund of Paid Fee):

11-1 Without prejudice to the provisions for withdrawing service applications and refunding fees stipulated in the table above, a submitted service application may be withdrawn and the paid fee partially refunded in accordance with the provisions mentioned below for some services marked with (**) in the table above. The withdrawal and fee refund do not apply to the remaining services.

11-2 The service applicant or their legal representative shall submit the withdrawal of the service application, based on a request submitted to the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> including the reasons for withdrawal, to be determined no later than the business day following the day the service application was submitted.

11-3 The withdrawal request shall be decided upon within two business days of its submission. The deadline for deciding on the request may be extended if the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> deems it necessary, taking into consideration that the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> has not yet begun to examine the subject of the service.

11-4 The paid fee shall be partially refunded if the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> approves the service withdrawal request, at a rate of 25% of the fee paid for some services listed in the schedule of fees.

## Appendix (2)

<table_caption>Appendix (2) Amendments</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Book | Article | Type of Amendment | Text after Amendment |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | The Third | 5-14 | Article Amendment | The Secretary <orig>أمين السر</orig> shall notify the Board of Commissioners <orig>مجلس المفوضين</orig> in writing of all decisions issued by the Disciplinary Board <orig>مجلس التأديب</orig> immediately upon their issuance. He shall also notify the concerned parties of the decisions issued against them within three business days from the date of their issuance, and he may use all approved means to send the notification. |
| 2 | The Third | 11-1 | Article Amendment | If the Complaints and Grievances Committee <orig>لجنة الشكاوى والتظلمات</orig> or the Disciplinary Board <orig>مجلس التأديب</orig>, during the review of a complaint or violation, deems it necessary to seek technical expertise in areas not prescribed to the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> in accordance with the law, either of them may request the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> to appoint an expert or a technical committee in the required field. The decision shall specify the task of the expert or the committee, a deadline for submitting the report, and a date for its discussion session. It shall also specify, when necessary, the amount to be deposited to cover expenses and fees, the party responsible for depositing it, and the specified deadline for the deposit. - The Secretary <orig>أمين السر</orig> shall notify the concerned parties of the decision to appoint the expert or the technical committee after their selection/appointment by the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> – within three business days. |
</table>

<br>The Authority may request – at any time after receiving the application – any additional documents or information if it deems it necessary.<br>In the event that the licensed person fails to submit the required documents and data within the period specified by the Authority without an excuse acceptable to the Authority, the application shall be considered null and void. | for the company, whether filed by or against it and its subsidiaries, and the amounts of such cases, if they can be estimated.<br>• A declaration and undertaking from the Chairman of the Board of Directors or his representative to comply with the controls specified in the Law and these Regulations and to not repeat the licensed person's violation, and any other undertakings specified by the Authority.<br>• Any other documents or information requested by the Authority to ensure that the licensed person meets the basic conditions stipulated in Article (1-7) of this Book.<br>2. The Authority shall decide on the resumption of the suspended or restricted activity of the licensed person within two months from the date of its receipt of the plan referred to in the preceding clause, complete with all required information and documents.<br>3. The Authority shall notify the licensed person of its decision to approve or reject the plan. In the event of the Authority's approval of the plan, the Authority shall issue a decision to resume the licensed person's activity that was subject to suspension or restriction, after payment of the prescribed fees. |
| 4 | Fifth | First | 1-19-1 | Amendment of the Article | An application to obtain the Authority's approval for effective control over a licensed person shall be submitted in accordance with the following procedures:<br>1. The application shall be submitted using the form in Appendix No. (11) of this Book, along with payment of the prescribed fees, at least (60) sixty days before entering into arrangements or agreements that would lead to effective control over the licensed person. The period shall be calculated from the date of completion of all required data and information.<br>2. The Authority shall decide on the application within a maximum period of (60) sixty days from the date of its submission, complete with any information or documents requested by the Authority. The Authority shall grant its approval of the application after ensuring that any effective control over the licensed person or ownership of its shares or capital stakes will not impede the supervision and oversight of the licensed person or lead to its non-compliance with the Law and these Regulations, and after the applicant has paid the prescribed fees. In the event that the Authority rejects the application, the rejection decision must be justified. | Provisions of the paragraph<br>A declaration and undertaking from the Chairman of the Board of Directors or his representative to comply with the controls specified in the Law and these Regulations and to not repeat the licensed person's violation, and any other undertakings specified by the Authority.<br>• Any other documents or information requested by the Authority to ensure that the licensed person meets the basic conditions stipulated in Article (1-7) of this Book.<br>2. The Authority shall decide on the resumption of the suspended or restricted activity of the licensed person within two months from the date of its receipt of the plan referred to in the preceding clause, complete with all required information and documents.<br>3. The Authority shall notify the licensed person of its decision to approve or reject the plan. In the event of the Authority's approval of the plan, the Authority shall issue a decision to resume the licensed person's activity that was subject to suspension or restriction, after payment of the prescribed fees. |
</table>

<page_start>17</page_start>
<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Application to Cancel a Financial Activity License",
  "document_date": "2025-04-06",
  "issue_number": 1733,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar", "en"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains instructions and a form for applying to cancel a license for financial securities activities, issued by the Capital Markets Authority of Kuwait."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1733 Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 H – 6/4/2025 AD
17
</header>

Instructions
- The licensed person shall fulfill all that is stated in Appendix (27) Instructions for the Application to Cancel Some or All Securities Activities Licenses.
- To apply for the cancellation of a license, prior approval from the Extraordinary General Assembly is required for the proposal to cancel some or all securities activities licenses, provided that this cancellation is justified.
- The licensed person shall adhere to the time periods stipulated in Book Five concerning the cancellation of the license at the request of the licensed person.
- The proposed date for cancellation shall be at least six months after the date of submitting the application.
- The Authority may request any additional information, documents, or clarifications from the licensed person during the review of their application. If they fail to provide the required documents and information within the period specified by the Authority in the notification without an excuse acceptable to the Authority, the application shall be considered null and void.
- The Authority shall decide on the application within two months of the fulfillment of all required documents and information.
- Provide the Authority with documents supporting the application in the event that any requirement in this form or the required attachments does not apply to the applicant.
- The applicant shall comply with all procedures issued by the Authority required after the decision on the application.
- Units subject to the supervision of the Central Bank <orig>البنك المركزي</orig> shall comply with the instructions for license cancellation regulated in the Memorandum of Understanding concluded between the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Central Bank <orig>البنك المركزي</orig>.
- The licensed person shall notify the Authority in writing immediately upon the occurrence of any obstacles in the procedures for canceling the securities activities license.
- The licensed person shall apply for license renewal in the event of non-compliance with the specified time periods for license cancellation.
- The Authority may compel the applicant for license cancellation to take all measures and precautions that ensure no harm is caused to the interests of its clients or the integrity of the financial system as a result of the license cancellation.
- The licensed person may resort to the Authority's arbitration system to settle disputes related to securities activities.
- The licensed person must submit the cancellation application through the Authority's electronic portal and pay the prescribed fees. In case of any inquiries regarding the submission of the application or related matters, contact the Licensing and Registration Department <orig>إدارة التراخيص والتسجيل</orig> at the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> at this address:
Kuwait – Sharq – Al Hamra Tower/Floor 20 – Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
P.O. Box 3913, Safat 13040, Kuwait
lrd@cma.gov.kw

## 2. Applicant's Information
### 1.2 Applicant's Information
Name of the Licensed Person
License Number
Proposed License Cancellation Date
### 2.2 Contact Officer's Information
Name
Telephone Number
Mobile Number (Individual)
Email

## 3. License to be Canceled
### 1.3 License to be Canceled
- ☐ Investment Portfolio Manager.
- ☐ Investment Advisor.
- ☐ Custodian.
- ☐ Investment Controller.
- ☐ Market Maker.
- ☐ Asset Valuator.
- ☐ Collective Investment Scheme Manager.
- ☐ Underwriter.
- ☐ Securities Broker registered with a securities exchange.
- ☐ Securities Broker not registered with a securities exchange.
- ☐ Qualified Securities Broker registered with a securities exchange.
- ☐ Credit Rating Agency.

# 4. Required Attachments and Documents

## 1.4 Required Attachments

<table_caption>Checklist of Required Documents for License Cancellation</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Required Attachment / Document | Attachment Status* | Notes |
|:---:|:---|:---|:---|
| | **Documents required when submitting the cancellation request** | | |
| 1 | Minutes of the extraordinary general assembly meeting indicating the shareholders' approval of the reasoned proposal to cancel the securities activities license. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 2 | The company's Board of Directors' resolution regarding the cancellation of the securities activities license. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 3 | A report from an auditor registered with the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 4 | A copy of the client register – in accordance with Clause (4) of the responsibilities of the Licensed Person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> as stated in Appendix (27). | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 5 | A copy of Form No. (2) of Appendix No. (2) Forms for Securities Investment Portfolios from Book Seven (Client Money and Assets) of the Executive Bylaws <orig>الكتاب السابع (أموال العملاء وأصولهم) من اللائحة التنفيذية</orig>. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 6 | Notification to the Central Bank of Kuwait <orig>بنك الكويت المركزي</orig> regarding the cancellation of all securities activities and the conversion to a finance company. | ☐ Available ☒ Not Applicable | |
| 7 | A copy of the fee payment receipt. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| | **The documents listed below are to be submitted in the event of a desire to liquidate the Licensed Person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig>** | | |
| 1 | Liquidator's <orig>المصفي</orig> details: <br> • Name of the Liquidator <orig>المصفي</orig>. <br> • A copy of the Liquidator's <orig>المصفي</orig> license / registration certificate. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 2 | Joint declaration between the Licensed Person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> and the Liquidator <orig>المصفي</orig> of independence and absence of conflict of interest. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
</table>

*If the attachment status is not applicable to the applicant, please provide the Authority with a separate letter explaining the reasons why it is not applicable.

Instructions
- Please fill out this form completely and ensure all attachments related to this form are included.
- This form is to be submitted by any entity wishing to enter into arrangements or agreements that lead to actual control over a licensed person in accordance with Article (1-19) of this Book.
- The applicant is obligated to pay the prescribed fees for the application for approval of actual control over a licensed person.
- A person subject to the provisions of Book Nine (Mergers and Acquisitions) of these bylaws is exempt from filling out this form.
- The prior approval of the Central Bank must be obtained for units subject to its supervision.
- Compliance with the rules of the stock exchange and the rules for trading unlisted securities at Boursa Kuwait <orig>بورصة الكويت</orig> must be observed.
- This form must be submitted at least 60 days prior to the date of commencing the actual control procedures.
- The Authority may request any additional information, documents, or clarifications from the applicant when reviewing the application.
- The applicant must send this form or any inquiries regarding its completion or related matters to the Licensing and Registration Department at the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> at this address:
Kuwait <orig>الكويت</orig> – Sharq <orig>شرق</orig> – Al Hamra Tower <orig>برج الحمراء</orig>/15th Floor – Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
P.O. Box 3913 Safat <orig>الصفاة</orig> 13040 Kuwait <orig>الكويت</orig>
lrd@cma.gov.kw

## 3. Integrity and Financial Soundness Criteria (for a Natural Person)*
1. Are you currently facing legal proceedings, or have you ever been convicted, locally or abroad, in cases related to a crime against honor or integrity, money laundering, terrorism financing, capital market crimes, or corruption crimes?
☐ Yes
☐ No
2. Have you ever, during your periods of employment, refused to comply with and adhere to the provisions of the law, regulatory requirements, and professional standards, or have you obstructed procedures, been misleading, or dishonest in cooperating with regulatory authorities?
☐ Yes
☐ No
3. Have you ever been convicted, had a penalty imposed on you, or had a disciplinary action issued against you by a professional or regulatory body?
☐ Yes
☒ No
4. Have you ever been dismissed from your position or job, or been prevented from applying for a vacant position or job in any entity?
☒ Yes
☐ No
5. Have you been a partner, whether in ownership, or held a position as a board member or an executive function for an entity whose application for registration or license to conduct business was rejected or canceled by the Authority or any other regulatory authorities?
☐ Yes
☐ No
6. Has any institution that you managed or held a position or executive function in ever been liquidated or declared bankrupt?
☐ Yes
☐ No
7. Have you ever defaulted on the payment of any debts owed by you to the banking or financial sector or any other entities, whether local or foreign?
☐ Yes
☐ No
8. Has a judgment ever been issued declaring your bankruptcy, whether in Kuwait or abroad?
☐ Yes
☐ No
9. Have you ever entered into a settlement with your creditors? And have you committed to its implementation, whether locally or abroad?
☐ Yes
☐ No
10. Do you hold shares in other companies exceeding 1% of their capital, whether locally or abroad?
☐ Yes

# 4. Declaration
* I acknowledge that I have reviewed the obligations stipulated in the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> Law No. 7 of 2010, its Executive Bylaws, and their amendments, as well as the regulations, resolutions, and instructions issued by the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>.
* I affirm the validity, accuracy, and completeness of the information provided in this form and its related attachments, and the truthfulness of the stated facts. I also acknowledge my awareness of the Authority's laws and regulations concerning penalties for submitting any incorrect or misleading information in this form or its related attachments.
* I undertake to notify the Authority of any changes that may occur to the information and data provided to the Authority related to this form.
* I acknowledge that I am aware of the right of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> to take any penal or disciplinary action against any person who submits incorrect and misleading data or declarations in this form.
* I acknowledge that I am aware that the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> may take any penal or disciplinary action against any person who submits incorrect and misleading data or declarations in this form. This serves as my acknowledgment and undertaking thereof...

<table>
| Applicant's Signature | |
|:---|:---|
| Applicant's Name | |
| Applicant's Capacity | |
| Signature | |
| Date | |
</table>

# 5. Required Attachments and Documents

## 1.4 Required Attachments

<table_caption>List of Required Attachments and Documents</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Required Attachment / Document | Attachment Status* | Notes |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | A precise and detailed investment plan clarifying the objective of the effective control, and information on the structural, financial, and administrative changes intended to be made in the licensed person, and the justifications for such changes. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 2 | A list of shareholders who have given preliminary approval for the sale and their ownership percentages. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 3 | Prior approval from the Central Bank if the applicant is one of the units subject to its supervision. | ☐ Available ☒ Not Applicable | |
| 4 | Approval from the applicant's Board of Directors (for a legal person). | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 5 | A copy of the Articles of Association, Memorandum of Association, and Commercial Register (for a legal person). | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 6 | A copy of the license certificate (for a licensed person). | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 7 | A copy of the Civil ID / a copy of the passport (for non-Kuwaitis) (for a natural person). | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 8 | A certificate of no criminal record (for a natural person). | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 9 | A legal opinion from the applicant's external legal advisor regarding lawsuits or a group of lawsuits with a material impact on the company's financial position, whether filed by or against it, or by or against its subsidiaries, and the amounts of such lawsuits if they can be estimated (for a legal person). | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 10 | The regulatory status of the applicant and the soundness of their financial position according to the financial statements for the last three years, after their approval by the regulatory authority. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
| 11 | A copy of the fee payment receipt. | ☐ Available ☐ Not Applicable | |
</table>

* If the attachment status is not applicable to the applicant, please provide the Authority with a separate letter explaining the reasons why it is not applicable.

# Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>

## Announcement

The owners of Al-Khuzami General Trading Company for Foodstuffs <orig>شركة الخزامي للتجارة العامة للمواد الغذائية</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation
have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry to dissolve and liquidate the company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection should present it to the Court of First Instance within thirty days from the date of this announcement's publication, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners, in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

## Announcement

The owners of Oshba Company for Selling Mobile Food <orig>شركة عشبة لبيع الأغذية المتنقلة</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation
have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry to dissolve and liquidate the company.
Legal Entity: One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection should present it to the Court of First Instance within thirty days from the date of this announcement's publication, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners, in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

## Announcement

Messrs./ Miska Company for Trading in All Medical Equipment and Supplies <orig>شركة مسكا للاتجار في جميع المعدات والمستلزمات الطبية</orig> has submitted a request to the Commercial Registry Department approved by the Ministry to register an agency, which has been registered under entry number: 2025/00260
Company and Nationality: Planer - United Kingdom
The agency's activity consists of: Incubators (excluding BT37 for human
IVF), controlled-rate freezers, cryogenic storage, cooling, and transport vessels, monitoring systems, tracking systems, CELL-TEK chambers, ZANDAIR devices.
The term shall be from: 07/05/2024 to: 07/05/2026

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-first Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - April 6, 2025 CE
25
</header>



<table_caption>Tender Details for Ministry of Information Practice</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice Subject | Requesting Entity | Fee for the Terms and Specifications Booklet | Date and Location for Opening Bids |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Providing technical services and solutions for digital systems | Information Systems Center | 75 K.D. | Day: Sunday, corresponding to: 20/4/2025, Tenders Section, Financial Affairs Department, 6th Floor, at 2:00 PM |
</table>

- The practice documents can be obtained starting from Sunday, 30/3/2025, and on the following days during the official working hours of the Financial Affairs Department (Ministry building located in the Rivi area – 6th Floor – Tenders Section). The deadline for submitting bids is Sunday, 20/4/2025, at 1:00 PM. Bids received after this deadline will not be considered. Please note that the aforementioned fees are non-refundable.
- All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, except for the bid form and the initial deposit, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- Bids shall be placed in the bid box at the Tenders Section, accompanied by an initial deposit of (1,400 K.D.) in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from an approved local bank in the State of Kuwait, unconditional and free of any reservations. It must be valid for the entire duration of the bid's validity, which is (90 days).
- All companies participating in the practice are invited to attend the opening of the envelopes at the time and place specified in the table above.

Note:
The practice documents may be collected by companies specialized in this field, provided they are registered with the Ministry's Tenders Section, from 9:00 AM to 1:00 PM, upon presentation of the 2025 registration card.
The Ministry's website for practices:
(https://tenders.awqaf.gov.kw/Tender/Tender_Public_Practice)

# Ministry of Islamic Affairs <orig>وزارة الشؤون الإسلامية</orig>
## Announcement
Regarding the issuance of Practice No. 52 for the year 2024/2025
Purchase of licenses for the Human Resources mechanization system and the mobile device fingerprint program
The Ministry of Islamic Affairs <orig>وزارة الشؤون الإسلامية</orig> announces the issuance of the following Practice No. 52-2024/2025:

<table_caption>Tender Details for Ministry of Islamic Affairs Practice No. 52/2024-2025</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Practice Subject | Requesting Entity | Fee for the Terms and Specifications Booklet | Date and Location for Opening Bids |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Purchase of licenses for the Human Resources mechanization system and the mobile device fingerprint program | Information Systems Center | 75 K.D. | Day: Sunday, corresponding to: 20/4/2025, Tenders Section, Financial Affairs Department, 6th Floor, at 2:00 PM |
</table>

- The practice documents can be obtained starting from Sunday, 30/3/2025, and on the following days during the official working hours of the Financial Affairs Department (Ministry building located in the Rivi area – 6th Floor – Tenders Section). The deadline for submitting bids is Sunday, 20/4/2025, at 1:00 PM. Bids received after this deadline will not be considered. Please note that the aforementioned fees are non-refundable.
- All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, except for the bid form and the initial deposit, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- Bids shall be placed in the bid box at the Tenders Section, accompanied by an initial deposit of (750 K.D.) in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from an approved local bank in the State of Kuwait, unconditional and free of any reservations. It must be valid for the entire duration of the bid's validity, which is (90 days).
- All companies participating in the practice are invited to attend the opening of the envelopes at the time and place specified in the table above.

Note:
The practice documents may be collected by companies specialized in this field, provided they are registered with the Ministry's Tenders Section, from 9:00 AM to 1:00 PM, upon presentation of the 2025 registration card.
The Ministry's website for practices:
(https://tenders.awqaf.gov.kw/Tender/Tender_Public_Practice)

## Announcement

have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry to carry out the following procedure:
Dissolution and liquidation of the company
### Legal Entity
Limited Liability Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the standard procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners (in the case of a general partnership or simple limited partnership only) towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

The submission of an objection results in the continued liability of the joint partners, in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

The submission of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners (in the case of a general or simple limited partnership only) towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on the objection.

<header>
40 Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733 Seventy-first Year Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - April 6, 2025 AD
</header>
Anyone with an objection must submit it to the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the standard procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection will result in the continued liability of the joint partners (in the case of a general partnership or simple limited partnership only) towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

The submission of an objection will result in the continued liability of the jointly liable partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig>, in the case of a general partnership or simple limited partnership <orig>التضامنية أو التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

# Kuwait International Bank "KIB"
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting for the Financial Year Ended 31 December 2024
The Extraordinary General Assembly of the shareholders of Kuwait International Bank (K.S.C.P.) "KIB" held its annual meeting at twelve o'clock in the morning on Thursday, March 20, 2025, on the tenth floor of the "KIB" main building.
The meeting was chaired by Mr. Mohammed Jarrah Al-Sabah <orig>محمد جراح الصباح</orig> - Chairman of the Board of Directors, with the attendance of:
- Mr. Raed Jawad Bukhamseen <orig>رائد جواد بوخمسين</orig> - Vice Chairman and CEO
- Mr. Mohamed Said El-Saka <orig>محمد سعيد السقا</orig> - Deputy CEO
- Sheikh Dr. Abdulaziz Khalifa Al-Qassar <orig>الشيخ د. عبدالعزيز خليفة القصار</orig> - Executive Member of the Sharia Supervisory Board
- Sheikh Khalid Hamdan Al-Dhafiri <orig>الشيخ خالد حمدان الظفيري</orig> - Representative of the External Sharia Audit Office
- Mr. Khalid Taher Al-Rasheed <orig>خالد طاهر الرشيد</orig> - Representative of the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
- Mr. Khalid Al-Omari <orig>خالد العمري</orig> - Representative of the Kuwait Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية للمقاصة</orig>
- The Bank's Auditors:-
- Mr. Talal Yousef Al-Muzaini <orig>طلال يوسف المزيني</orig> - Deloitte & Touche - Al-Wazzan & Co.
- Mr. Bader Adel Al-Abduljader <orig>بدر عادل العبدالجادر</orig> - Ernst & Young - Al-Aiban, Al-Osaimi & Partners
- Shareholders via:-
A. Electronic attendance with 261,019,440 shares, representing 16.546% (electronic voting percentage) of the total authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital of the Bank, after excluding treasury shares.
B. In-person attendance, representing in person and by proxy, with 948,336,020 shares, representing 60.117% (in-person attendance percentage) of the total authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital of the Bank, after excluding treasury shares.
- The total number of shares present (electronically and in-person) is 1,209,355,460 shares, with an attendance rate of 76.663% of the total authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital of the Bank, after excluding treasury shares.
After the Chairman of the Extraordinary General Assembly announced that the legal quorum for the meeting was met, the items on the agenda were discussed and the following decisions were made:
1- Approval was granted to increase the Bank's authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital from an amount of 170,337,838.900 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (one hundred seventy million, three hundred thirty-seven thousand, eight hundred thirty-eight Kuwaiti Dinars and 900 fils) to# National Investments Company K.S.

**Text after amendment:**
The authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital of the bank is set at an amount of 178,854,730.800 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (one hundred seventy-eight million, eight hundred fifty-four thousand, seven hundred thirty Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> and 800 fils <orig>فلس</orig>), divided into 1,788,547,308 shares (one billion, seven hundred eighty-eight million, five hundred forty-seven thousand, three hundred eight shares), with a nominal value of 100 fils <orig>فلس</orig> (one hundred fils <orig>فلس</orig>) per share, and all shares are cash shares.

# Watani Investment Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>, and Watani Financial Brokerage Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>
whereby Watani Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig> is the merging company and Watani Financial Brokerage Company <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية</orig> is the merged company, and all its annexes, including the consultation of the independent investment advisor, the asset valuation report prepared by the independent asset valuator, and the share exchange ratio, after obtaining the approvals of the relevant regulatory authorities.

**Second Item:**
Approval was granted for the merger by amalgamation between Watani Investment Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig> and Watani Financial Brokerage Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>, whereby Watani Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig> will be the merging company and Watani Financial Brokerage Company <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية</orig> will be the merged company through the dissolution of the merged company, in accordance with the provisions of Law No. (7) of 2010 and its executive regulations, and their amendments, after obtaining the approvals of the relevant regulatory authorities.

**Third Item:**
Approval was granted for the dissolution of Watani Financial Brokerage Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig> and the transfer of its financial liability by amalgamation (assets and liabilities) with all its assets, rights, and obligations to Watani Investment Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>. Consequently, the legal personality of Watani Financial Brokerage Company <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية</orig> will be extinguished upon completion of the merger procedures, and it will be struck off and its licenses canceled from the records of the Public Shareholding Companies Department at the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>, in accordance with the provisions of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and its executive regulations, and their amendments, and Law No. (1) of 2016 issuing the Companies Law and its executive regulations, and their amendments.
Accordingly, Mr. Tariq Abdul Latif Al-Shehab <orig>طارق عبد اللطيف الشهاب</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors, announced the end of the meeting at 12:30 PM.

Chairman of the Board of Directors

# Arkan Al Kuwait Real Estate Company <orig>شركة أركان الكويت العقارية</orig>
## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting for the Fiscal Year Ended October 31, 2024
The meeting was held on Tuesday, March 18, 2025, at 11:00 AM at the headquarters of Arkan Al Kuwait Real Estate Company <orig>شركة أركان الكويت العقارية</orig> – located in the Sharq area <orig>منطقة الشرق</orig> – Block 8 – Al-Shuhada Street – Al Hamra Business Tower <orig>برج الحمراء التجاري</orig> – 66th Floor. The legal quorum was met with the presence of representatives for 203,376,001 shares out of 251,149,622 shares, representing 80.978% of the capital shares, and in the presence of:
1- Mr. Abdulrahman Hamad Al-Turkait <orig>عبدالرحمن حمد التركيت</orig>, Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer
2- Mr. Yasser Mohammed Al-Natour <orig>ياسر محمد الناطور</orig>, Executive Director of Support Services
3- Mr. Anas Ali Owaidat <orig>أنس علي عويدات</orig>, Senior Manager of the Finance Department
4- Mr. Mohammed Al-Tahoul <orig>محمد الطحول</orig>, representing the company's auditors, (Grant Thornton) Al-Qatami, Al-Aiban & Partners <orig>(جرانت ثورينتون ) القطامي والعيبان وشركاهم</orig>.
5- Mr. Abdullah Abdulrahman <orig>عبدالله عبدالرحمن</orig>, authorized representative of Al-Mashora & Al-Raya for Islamic Financial Consulting Company <orig>شركة المشورة والراية للاستشارات المالية الاسلامية</orig>
The Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer opened the session at 11:30 AM and welcomed the esteemed shareholders and attendees, and

## Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
### Dated 25/3/2025

At 12:45 PM on Tuesday, 25/3/2025, the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was held at the company's headquarters. After the legal quorum was met with the attendance of a number of shareholders owning and representing [191,944,794] shares out of the company's total shares of [220,500,000], which is a rate of 87.049%, and after reviewing the agenda, the following was approved:

1- Approval to increase the company's issued and paid-up capital from KWD 22,050,000 to KWD 23,600,000, by issuing 15,500,000 shares equivalent to KWD 1,550,000 at a value of (100) fils per share, at a rate of 7.029478%, to be distributed as free bonus shares to the shareholders registered in the company's records as of the end of the record date, according to the timeline in the disclosure form for share entitlements, and to authorize the Board of Directors to dispose of fractional shares resulting from the distribution of the free bonus shares as it deems appropriate.
2- Approval to amend Article (6) of the Memorandum of Association and Article (7) of the Articles of Association as follows:

**Text before amendment:**
The authorized capital of the company is set at KWD 30,000,000 (thirty million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), divided into 300,000,000 shares, with a value of (100 fils) per share, and all shares are in cash. The issued and paid-up capital of the company is set at KWD 22,050,000 (twenty-two million and fifty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), divided into 220,500,000 shares, with a value of (100) fils per share, and all shares are in cash.

**Text after amendment:**
The authorized capital of the company is set at KWD 30,000,000 (thirty million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), divided into 300,000,000 shares, with a value of (100 fils) per share, and all shares are in cash. The issued and paid-up capital of the company is set at KWD 23,600,000 (twenty-three million and six hundred thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>), divided into 236,000,000 shares, with a value of (100) fils per share, and all shares are in cash.

Subject to the approval of the competent regulatory authorities.
The meeting was adjourned at 1:00 PM.

Chairman of the Board of Directors

The discussion then moved to the following agenda:
- Adding a new clause to Article 47 of the company's Articles of Association to read as follows:
  - **Text of Article 47 before amendment:**
    First: A deduction of (10%) ten percent shall be allocated to the statutory reserve account. The General Assembly may suspend this deduction if the reserve exceeds half of the company's capital.
    Second: A deduction of (1%) shall be allocated to the Kuwait Foundation for the Advancement of Sciences <orig>مؤسسة الكويت للتقدم العلمي</orig>.
    Third: A percentage shall be deducted and allocated to the optional reserve account, as proposed by the Board of Directors and approved by the General Assembly. This deduction may be suspended by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly upon the proposal of the Board of Directors.
    Fourth: A portion of the profits shall be deducted, upon the proposal of the Board of Directors and as decided by the General Assembly, to meet the company's obligations under labor laws, and these funds may not be distributed to shareholders.
    Fifth: The amount necessary to distribute a first dividend of (5%) five percent to the shareholders shall be deducted, as determined by the Board of Directors and decided by the General Assembly.
    Sixth: After the foregoing, an amount decided by the Ordinary General Assembly, not exceeding (10%) ten percent of the remainder, shall be deducted and allocated for the remuneration of the Board of Directors.
    Seventh: The remainder of the profits shall then be distributed to the shareholders as an additional dividend, or carried forward to the next year upon the proposal of the Board of Directors, or allocated to establish a general reserve fund or an extraordinary depreciation fund.
  - **Text of Article 47 after amendment:**
    First: A deduction of (10%) ten percent shall be allocated to the statutory reserve account. The General Assembly may suspend this deduction if the reserve exceeds half of the company's capital.
    Second: A deduction of (1%) shall be allocated to the Kuwait Foundation for the Advancement of Sciences <orig>مؤسسة الكويت للتقدم العلمي</orig>.
    Third: A percentage shall be deducted and allocated to the optional reserve account, as proposed by the Board of Directors and approved by the General Assembly. This deduction may be suspended by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly upon the proposal of the Board of Directors.
    Fourth: A portion of the profits shall be deducted, upon the proposal of the Board of Directors and as decided by the General Assembly, to meet the company's obligations under labor laws, and these funds may not be distributed to shareholders.
    Fifth: The amount necessary to distribute a first dividend of (5%) five percent to the shareholders shall be deducted, as determined by the Board of Directors and decided by the General Assembly.
    Sixth: After the foregoing, an amount decided by the Ordinary General Assembly, not exceeding (10%) ten percent of the remainder, shall be deducted and allocated for the remuneration of the Board of Directors.
    Seventh: The remainder of the profits shall then be distributed to the shareholders as an additional dividend, or carried forward to the next year upon the proposal of the Board of Directors, or allocated to establish a general reserve fund or an extraordinary depreciation fund.
    Eighth: The Ordinary General Assembly may, upon the proposal of the Board of Directors, distribute profits to the shareholders at the end of the fiscal year, or on a semi-annual basis. It may also, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly to be renewed annually, pre-authorize the Board of Directors to distribute profits on a semi-annual basis and to determine the timeline for this distribution, provided that such distribution is from actual profits, in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles, and does not affect the company's paid-up capital."
    The meeting concluded at 11:15 AM.

Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer

And they have approved the following:
Ratification of the minutes of the previous agenda, which was approved and ratified.
Item One: Amendment of Article No. 29 of the Memorandum of Association <orig>عقد التاسيس</orig> and the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>.
### Text of Article 29 of the Articles of Association before the amendment:
- The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall elect, by secret ballot, a Chairman of the Board <orig>رئيسا للمجلس</orig> and a Vice Chairman <orig>نائبا للرئيس</orig>. The Chairman of the Board of Directors shall represent the company in its relations with third parties and before the judiciary, in addition to the other competencies specified in the contract. His signature shall be considered as the signature of the Board of Directors in the company's relationship with third parties. He must implement the Board's decisions and adhere to its recommendations. The Vice Chairman shall replace him in his absence or if he is prevented from exercising his competencies.
### Text of Article 29 after the amendment:
- The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall elect, by secret ballot, a Chairman of the Board <orig>رئيسا للمجلس</orig> and a Vice Chairman <orig>نائبا للرئيس</orig>. The Chairman of the Board of Directors shall represent the company in its relations with third parties and before the judiciary, in addition to the other competencies specified in the contract. His signature shall be considered as the signature of the Board of Directors in the company's relationship with third parties. He must implement the Board's decisions and adhere to its recommendations. The Vice Chairman shall replace him in his absence or if he is prevented from exercising his competencies.
The Board of Directors shall have the broadest powers to manage the company and to carry out all actions required for the management of the company in accordance with its objectives. This authority shall only be limited by what is stipulated in the law, these articles, or the resolutions of the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>. The Board of Directors may borrow, sell, and mortgage the company's real estate, provide guarantees, engage in arbitration, conciliation, and donations, and open and close bank accounts.
The amendment to the text of the article was discussed and approved by all attendees.
In conclusion, the Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> thanked the attendees and concluded the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> meeting at exactly two o'clock in the afternoon.
Chairman of the Board of Directors

## Kuwait International Takaful Insurance Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية العالمية للتأمين التكافلي</orig>
### Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting <orig>محضر اجتماع الجمعية العمومية غير العادية</orig>
### Held on 23/3/2025

The Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية غير العادية</orig> of the Kuwait International Takaful Insurance Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية العالمية للتأمين التكافلي</orig> convened at the company's headquarters located on Arabian Gulf Street, Ahmed Tower, at 11:00 AM on Sunday, 23/03/2025, with a quorum of 100%. The General Assembly meeting was chaired by the company's Chairman of the Board of Directors, with the attendance of:
1. Mr. Ghanem Mez'al Fahad Al-Shammari <orig>غانم مزعل فهد الشمري</orig>, Chairman of the Board of Directors
2. Mr. Abdulaziz Saud Al-Mutairi <orig>عبدالعزيز سعود المطيري</orig>, Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors
3. Mrs. Sahar Majed Faour <orig>سحر ماجد فاعور</orig>, Secretary
4. Mr. Fahad Abdulrahman Al-Bediwi <orig>فهد عبدالرحمن البديوي</orig>, Gulf Clearing Company <orig>الخليجية لحفظ الأوراق المالية</orig>

The General Assembly has ratified the following items:

### 1 - Amendment of Article No. (14) of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>:
**Text before amendment:**
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> composed of (3) three members, of whom the entity or entities entitled to appoint representatives to the Board of Directors shall appoint a number proportionate to their shareholding in the company, and the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> shall elect the remaining members by secret ballot.

**Text after amendment:**
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> composed of (5) five members, of whom the entity or entities entitled to appoint representatives to the Board of Directors shall appoint a number proportionate to their shareholding in the company, and the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> shall elect the remaining members by secret ballot.

### 2 - Amendment of the text of Article No. (5) of the Memorandum of Association <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article No. (4) of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>:
(In accordance with Ministerial Resolution No. 167 of 2022 regarding the regularization of companies' statuses according to the United Nations International Standard Industrial Classification of All Economic Activities).

**Text before amendment:**
The purposes of the company are: The purposes of the company shall be as set out below, provided that all the company's transactions are subject to the provisions of the law in accordance with the rulings of Islamic Sharia <orig>الشريعة الإسلامية</orig>, and in a manner that does not conflict with the organizing laws and resolutions.
1. Fire insurance.
2. Accident insurance.
3. Marine and aviation insurance.
4. Engineering insurance (equipment, machinery, devices, and electronics).
5. Motor insurance (compulsory / supplementary).
6. Civil liability insurance towards third parties or third-party property.
7. Health insurance (for a period of two years) covering treatment expenses and surgical operations.

The company shall engage in all cooperative Takaful insurance <orig>التأمين التكافلي</orig> activities and related matters, and any activity required for its practice, and carry out insurance and reinsurance business, enter into all contracts, and perform all legal actions it deems necessary to achieve its purposes.
To invest all or part of the company's movable or immovable funds in the various fields it deems appropriate, in a manner that does not conflict with the organizing laws and resolutions related to insurance.
To provide consultations and conduct technical studies in the field of insurance and insurance management for companies or others interested in the field of Takaful insurance <orig>التأمين التكافلي</orig>.
To own and acquire the right of disposal over all movable and immovable property, or any part thereof, or any privileges that the company believes are necessary and appropriate for the nature of its business and essential for the growth of its funds.
The company shall have the right to conduct the aforementioned business in the State of Kuwait and abroad, either as a principal or as an agent. The company may have an interest in or participate in any way with entities that engage in similar activities or that may assist it in achieving its purposes in Kuwait or abroad, and it may purchase or affiliate with these entities.

**Text after amendment:**
The purposes of the company shall be as set out below, provided that all the company's transactions are subject to the provisions of the law in accordance with the rulings of Islamic Sharia <orig>الشريعة الإسلامية</orig>, and in a manner that does not conflict with the organizing laws and resolutions, and what is required to preserve the objective of achieving cooperation and solidarity among the participants.

<table_caption>Company Activity Codes and Descriptions</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Activity Code | Activity Name |
|:--|:---|:---|
| 1 | 651107 | Non-life Takaful insurance and fund formation. |
| 2 | 681091 | Owning real estate and movables for the benefit of the company. |
| 3 | 649918 | Investing financial surpluses by investing them in financial portfolios managed by specialized companies and entities. |
| 4 | 649917 | Buying and selling shares and bonds for the company's account. |
| 5 | 660004 | Providing administrative and technical services to insurance companies. |
</table>

### 3 - Amendment of Article No. (25) of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>:
**Text before amendment:**
- Without prejudice to the provisions of Companies Law <orig>قانون الشركات</orig> No. 25 of 2012 and its regulations

- Without prejudice to the provisions of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 and its Executive Regulations, the Ordinary General Assembly shall determine the remuneration of the members of the Board of Directors.
Text after amendment:
- Without prejudice to the provisions of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 and its Executive Regulations, the Ordinary General Assembly shall determine the remuneration of the members of the Board of Directors.

4 – Amendment of Article No. (29) of the Articles of Association, Clause No. 4:
Text before amendment:
- Any of the modern means of communication specified in the Executive Regulations of Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 and its amendments. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> must be notified in writing of the agenda, time, and place of the meeting at least seven days before it is held, for its representative to attend.
Text after amendment:
- Any of the modern means of communication specified in the Executive Regulations of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 and its amendments. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> must be notified in writing of the agenda, time, and place of the meeting at least seven days before it is held, for its representative to attend.

5 – Amendment of Article No. (36) of the Articles of Association:
Text before amendment:
The Annual General Assembly shall convene upon the invitation of the Board of Directors within the three months following the end of the fiscal year, at the time and place designated by the Board of Directors. The Board may call the General Assembly to convene whenever necessary. The Board of Directors must call the Assembly to convene upon a reasoned request from a number of shareholders holding ten percent of the company's capital, or upon the request of the auditor, within fifteen days from the date of the request. The agenda shall be prepared by the party calling for the meeting.
The procedures for inviting the General Assembly, the quorum for attendance, and voting shall be subject to the provisions for the Constituent Assembly as stipulated in Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 and its amendments.
Text after amendment:
The Annual General Assembly shall convene upon the invitation of the Board of Directors within the three months following the end of the fiscal year, at the time and place designated by the Board of Directors. The Board may call the General Assembly to convene whenever necessary. The Board of Directors must call the Assembly to convene upon a reasoned request from a number of shareholders holding ten percent of the company's capital, or upon the request of the auditor, within fifteen days from the date of the request. The agenda shall be prepared by the party calling for the meeting.
The procedures for inviting the General Assembly, the quorum for attendance, and voting shall be subject to the provisions for the Constituent Assembly as stipulated in Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 and its amendments.

6 – Amendment of Article No. (51) of the Articles of Association:
Text before amendment:
The company shall be dissolved for any of the reasons stipulated in Companies Law No. 25 of 2012, its amendments, and its Executive Regulations.
Text after amendment:
The company shall be dissolved for any of the reasons stipulated in Companies Law No. 1 of 2016, its amendments, and its Executive Regulations.

7 – Amendment of Article No. (52) of the Articles of Association:
Text before amendment:
The liquidation of the company shall be carried out in the manner specified in the provisions of Companies Law No. 25 of 2012, its amendments, and its Executive Regulations.
Text after amendment:
The liquidation of the company shall be carried out in the manner specified in the provisions of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016, its amendments, and its Executive Regulations.

8 – Amendment of Article No. (53) of the Articles of Association:
Text before amendment:
The provisions of Commercial Companies Law No. 25 of 2012, its amendments, and its Executive Regulations shall apply to all matters for which no special provision is made in the Memorandum of Association or in these Articles.
Text after amendment:
The provisions of Commercial Companies Law No. 1 of 2016, its amendments, and its Executive Regulations shall apply to all matters for which no special provision is made in the Memorandum of Association or in these Articles.
After reviewing and discussing the items on the agenda, the preceding resolutions and amendments were adopted and unanimously approved.
At the conclusion of the meeting, the Chairman of the Board of Directors and CEO thanked the attendees, and the proceedings of the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting were concluded at twelve o'clock noon on the same day.

Chairman of the Board of Directors

**Donia Holding Company (K.S.C.) Closed**
**Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting**

The Extraordinary General Assembly of the shareholders of Donia Holding Company <orig>شركة دنيا القابضة</orig> – a Kuwaiti Shareholding Company (Holding) – held its extraordinary meeting to add a new article to the company's Articles of Association, at 10:45 AM on Monday, March 24, 2025, at the company's headquarters located in Shuwaikh Industrial 3 <orig>الشويخ الصناعية الثالثة</orig> – Block A – Plot 98 – Mezzanine.
The meeting was chaired by Mr. Ali Abdulhameed Ali Al-Qattan <orig>علي عبد الحميد علي القطان</orig> – Deputy Chairman of the Board of Directors and CEO.
The meeting was also attended by:
- Mr. Fahad Abdulrahman Al-Bediwi <orig>فهد عبد الرحمن البديوي</orig> – representing the Gulf Clearing Company <orig>الشركة الخليجية لحفظ الأوراق المالية</orig>.
- Mr. Qusai Abdulhameed Al-Qattan <orig>قصي عبد الحميد القطان</orig> – in his capacity as Secretary of the Board.
- Shareholders holding 21,000,000 shares in person and by proxy, representing 100% of the company's total paid-up capital of 21,000,000 shares.
After announcing that the legal quorum for the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting was met, the Chairman opened the meeting by welcoming the attendees. He then proceeded to present the items on the agenda of the Extraordinary General Assembly. Accordingly, after reviewing the agenda, the following resolution was passed:
- It was approved to add a new article to the company's Articles of Association, to become Article No. (76), with the following text:
A shareholder's right to dispose of their shares shall be restricted by the following two conditions:
1- The stipulation of a right of first refusal for the company's shareholders to purchase shares that their owner wishes to sell.
2- The stipulation of the Board of Directors' approval of the share purchaser.
The transactions referred to in Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 are exempted from these two restrictions.

3- Before disposing of his shares, the shareholder must notify the company of the terms of sale. The disposal of shares shall not be effective until ten days have passed from the date of notification without any of the shareholders submitting a request to purchase the shares. If a shareholder comes forward to purchase the shares, it must be at the price stated in the terms of sale.
4- Without prejudice to the provisions related to the company's purchase of its own shares, if the Board of Directors rejects the person of the buyer, it must purchase the shares for the company's account within ten days from the date the Board of Directors was notified of the approval request. In this case, the purchase shall be at the price at which the shareholder agreed to sell his shares.

# Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>
Re-issuance of Practice No. M/2024/31-2025
The Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> announces the issuance of a (public) practice for the rental of 20 half-lorries with drivers and handling workers, in accordance with the terms and technical specifications in the practice documents.
General Guidelines for the Practice:
1- The practice is (public) for practitioners accredited by the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>.
2- Applicants for this practice must be institutions/companies specialized in the work subject of the practice within Kuwait <orig>الكويت</orig>, registered in the Commercial Register and the Kuwait <orig>الكويت</orig> Chamber of Commerce and Industry for the current year. A certificate to this effect, dated concurrently with the practice issuance date, must be attached to the bid.
3- This practice is (indivisible), and the bidder is not entitled to submit alternative offers.
4- The fee for obtaining a copy of the practice documents is (75) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only.
5- The bid must be accompanied by a preliminary deposit of not less than (KD 2,000) two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only. This deposit must be in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee from a bank accredited in the State of Kuwait, issued in the name of the bidder and for the benefit of the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>, and must be unconditional. Bids not accompanied by this deposit, or accompanied by a deposit that violates any of the aforementioned controls, will be disregarded. The deposit must be valid for the required bid validity period.
6- The total duration of the contract is three months from the date of signing the contract, during which the contractor is obligated to execute the practice works in accordance with the general and special conditions, provisions, and technical specifications contained in the practice documents.
7- The bidder agrees that their bid shall remain valid and in effect, irrevocable, and cannot be withdrawn from the time of its submission until the end of its validity period. No price reduction will be accepted after the bid has been submitted.
8- If, upon studying the practice, the practitioner finds any error, deficiency, or discrepancy in the technical documents or bills of quantities that affects the bid categories or the value of the works, they must seek clarification from the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> before submitting their bid. The Ministry will study these comments and inquiries, answer them, and correct any error, deficiency, discrepancy, or conflict (if any). This shall not result in any additional liability or obligation on the part of the Ministry.
9- The practice documents shall be deposited in the bid box at the Supplies and Warehouses Department in the South Subhan <orig>صبحان الجنوبي</orig> area during official working hours, no later than (10) ten days from the date of the announcement, at exactly (12:00 noon), according to the decision issued by the Ministry regarding changing or extending the closing date. No bid received after the scheduled closing time will be accepted, nor will any amendment to the prices of submitted bids be considered after the bid has been submitted.
10- The practitioner must fill in the attached tables and provide a statement of all supplies necessary for the execution of the works subject of the practice – if any – within the same bid documents submitted. The Ministry has the right not to accept the bid if it does not include the completion of the tables in accordance with the public interest, with the need to adhere to the technical specifications and conditions of the practice.
11- The practitioner must submit all bank guarantees related to this practice in the Arabic language.
12- A preliminary meeting will be held five days after the announcement.

***

# Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
## Notice
Regarding the extension of the closing date for the Practice
No. (M.Sh.L 205 / 2024-2025)
Supply, installation, operation, inspection, and maintenance of a sewage treatment unit on the islands of Qaruh and Umm Al-Maradim <orig>جزيرتي قاروه وام المرادم</orig> for the General Directorate of Construction and Maintenance <orig>الإدارة العامة للإنشاءات والصيانة</orig> – Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
Please be advised that the closing date (bid submission) for the aforementioned practice has been extended to Wednesday, 7/5/2025 – at the Bid Opening Committee of the Purchasing Committee at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> building (Sharq area <orig>منطقة شرق</orig> – Al-Siddiq School – First Floor) from 8:00 AM until 1:00 PM. No bids submitted before or after the specified time will be accepted.

***
