# Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>
## Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department – Medical Supplies Control) announces the following tenders:

<table_caption>Tender for Medical Supplies</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Tender No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:---:|:---:|:---|:---:|:---|
| 1 | 5ANF02 | Medical consumables for the Anesthesia and Intensive Care Unit for Al-Farwaniya Hospital <orig>مستشفى الفروانية</orig> | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 2 | 5CS003 | Non-sterile cotton balls for the needs of sterilization departments in all hospitals | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 3 | 5CS004 | X-ray detectable gauze padding, size 20cm*50cm, for the needs of sterilization departments in all hospitals | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 4 | 5CS005 | Paper sterilization bags, size 140mm * 50mm * 330mm, for the needs of sterilization departments in all hospitals | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 5 | 5CS007 | Paper sterilization bags, size 90mm*50mm*150mm, for the needs of sterilization departments in all hospitals | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 6 | 5CS008 | Transparent sterilization rolls, size 300mm * 200m, for the needs of sterilization departments in all hospitals | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 7 | 5DB012 | Size 21 needles for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 8 | 5MEK01 | PICC LINE consumables for the Kuwait Cancer Control Center <orig>مركز الكويت لمكافحة السرطان</orig> | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
| 9 | 5TX001 | Postpartum maternity pads for the needs of all departments in specialized centers and hospitals | 75 | 30 days or more from the date of announcement |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the tender box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
Companies wishing to participate in the tender must meet the following conditions:
1 – The local company must be registered in the Supplier Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>.
2 – The local company must be specialized in the medical field, documented by a certified certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3 – When submitting two offers, two separate tender booklets must be purchased with two different receipts.
4 – Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Botanical Drugs <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنياتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and the product's registration in the Supplier Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, within the contents of the submitted bid (specific to Drug Control).
5 – Provide samples of new materials, whether it is a new product being requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, to the relevant control department (Medicines – Medical Supplies).
6 – Attach a National Labor Support Percentage Certificate <orig>شهادة نسبة دعم العمالة الوطنية</orig>.
7 – Tender documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8 – Fees for purchasing the tender booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the tender documents.
9 – Price quotations must be submitted in a sealed envelope, inclusive of the tender documents, by the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.

Companies wishing to participate in the tender must meet the following conditions:
1- The local company must be registered in the Suppliers Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field, documented by a certified certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two separate tender booklets must be purchased with two different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Botanical Drugs <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنياتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and the product's registration in the Suppliers Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, within the contents of the submitted bid (specific to Pharmaceuticals Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).
5- Provide samples of new materials, whether it is a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, to the relevant control department (Pharmaceuticals – Medical Supplies).
6- Attach a national labor support percentage certificate.
7- Tender documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.
8- The fee for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the tender documents.
9- Price quotations must be submitted in a sealed envelope, including the tender documents, by the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> website.

---

## Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee, Session No. 9/2025, held on 16/3/2025

After reviewing the applications submitted to amend data in the births and deaths records, it was decided to make the amendments listed below in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>). If the Committee does not receive any objection within fifteen days from the date of this announcement's publication, the amendment will be made in the records, and birth or death certificates will be issued according to the following amendment:

The Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>, stipulated in Article 15 of Law No. 36/69 and formed by Ministerial Resolution No. 1650/2021, has convened.
Mr. / Director of the Central Registry of Births and Deaths <orig>إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد والوفيات</orig>, as Chairman
Dr. / Head of the General Medical Council <orig>المجلس الطبي العام</orig>, as Member
Mr. / Head of the Research and Opinion Department, as Member
Mr. / Head of the Registration Department, as Member
Mr. / Head of the Deaths Department, as Member
Mr. / The Legal Researcher, as Member
Mr. / Head of the Records Department, as Member
The secretarial duties of the committee were performed by Mrs. / Alyaa Al-Saffar <orig>علياء الصفار</orig>.

The Committee reviewed applications from No. ((115)) to No. ((127)) in the attached list, concerning the amendment of data in the births and deaths records for requests of unrecorded births and deaths, amendments, and requests in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) for two consecutive issues. If the legal period (fifteen days) from the date of the last announcement expires without any objection being submitted, the amendments will be made in the registers, and birth and death certificates will be issued.
Therefore, after its review and ensuring the completion of all documents and records, the Committee has decided to announce the amendments.

Head of the Research and Opinion Department Head of the Registration Department Head of the Deaths Department
Committee Secretary Head of the General Medical Council <orig>رئيس المجلس الطبي العام</orig>
The Legal Researcher
Director of the Central Registry of Births

## Penal Judgment Announcement
The Court of First Instance, in its session held on 09-03-2021, issued a judgment in Case No. 20/006131 - Court of First Instance, Municipal Misdemeanors and Violations
Police Station No.: (17/0016701 - Municipality)
Automated Case No.: 202345860
Against the defendant: Ibrahim Kalayil Lanil <orig>إبراهيم كالائيل لانيل</orig>
Nationality: India, Civil ID No.: 285031104234
An in-absentia judgment was issued, ruling: To fine the defendant the sum of one hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> for the charges against him.
The Public Prosecution hereby notifies the convicted person of this judgment and instructs all security authorities to execute it in accordance with the provisions of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedure and Trials. It is noted that if a period of thirty-seven days, calculated from the day following publication, elapses without the convicted person filing an opposition or an appeal, the judgment will become final and enforceable against him.
Director of the Criminal Enforcement Prosecution

{
  "page_title": "Announcements of Real Estate Sale by Public Auction <orig>إعلانات عن بيع عقار بالمزاد العلني</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-04-06",

  "page_summary": "This page contains two public auction announcements for real estate properties, detailing the case numbers, property descriptions, auction terms, and legal notices."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
63
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
</header>


Against:
1- Bishra Thaqeel Rashid Al-Ajmi <orig>بشرى ثقيل راشد العجمي</orig>.
2- Ahmed Abd Sultan Shalash <orig>احمد عبد سلطان شلاش</orig>.
3- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.
4- Director of the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>مدير إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig>, in his capacity.
Property Description (according to the attached description certificate)
The property of Document No. 2016/5826, located in the Al-Nuaim <orig>النعيم</orig> area – Plot (227), Block No. (1), Plan M/37704 – with an area of 400 m², to be sold at public auction with a base price of KWD 420,000 (Four hundred and twenty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** And according to what is stated in the description certificate:
Private residence consisting of a ground floor, first floor, and a partial second floor. There is an unlicensed elevator, and a violation report No. 5431 was issued on 1/2/2024. The violation is still outstanding. This is for your information.
** And according to what is stated in the description certificate:
The disputed property located in the Al-Nuaim <orig>النعيم</orig> area – Block 1 – Street 18 – Plot 227
- House 3 at the time of inspection is as follows:
- The disputed property is a residential plot located on a single dead-end street, bordered by neighbors on 3 sides, and consists of two and a half floors with a white mosaic facade.
- Standard interior finishes.
- The total area of the property is 400 m² according to the document.
- The property's air conditioning is partially central and partially standard units.
- There is an elevator in the plot.
- Ground Floor: Reception hall with a bathroom and washbasins – living room – diwaniya with a bathroom and washbasins – driver's room – room with a bathroom – prep kitchen – main kitchen.
- First Floor: Master bedroom with a bathroom and dressing room – 4 rooms with two bathrooms – prep kitchen – living room open to the hallway.
- Half floor with the roof: Room – bathroom – prep kitchen – hall
Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction begins at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Department at the Ministry of Justice.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at their liability on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those initiating the sale procedures and at their own responsibility, without the Clerks Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in their favor for a similar rent."
President of the Court of First Instance

---

# Announcement of a Property Sale by Public Auction
The Clerks Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale by public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 1/5/2025 – Hall 52 – on the second floor of the Justice Palace at 9:00 AM – in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 2024/39 Sales/3
Filed by:
First: Maryam Ahmed Ali Al-Kandari <orig>مريم أحمد على الكندري</orig>.
Second: Siddiqa Ahmed Ali Al-Kandari <orig>صديقة أحمد على الكندري</orig>.

1- Maryam Fardh Khadlak <orig>مريم فرض خدلك</orig>.

5- Sharifa Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>شريفه أحمد على حسن الكندري</orig>.
6- Sarah Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>ساره أحمد على حسن الكندري</orig>.
7- Suad Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>سعاد أحمد على حسن الكندري</orig>.
8- The heirs of the late Ali Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>على أحمد على حسن الكندري</orig>.

<header>
Kuwait Today, Issue 1733, Seventy-first Year
64
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
</header>

First: Property Description: According to the attached description certificate.
- Property of Document No. 2023/6769 located in Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig> - Plot 279 - Block 4 - from Plan No. M/36912 - with an area of 400 m2.

*Inspection:*
- The disputed property is located in the Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig> area, Block 4, Street 16, House 38. The inspection was conducted as follows:
- The property subject of the lawsuit is a government house consisting of two floors, located on a single street with front and back access. On the other side is a dirt yard. The house's cladding is yellow stone. It is bordered by a neighbor on the right and a neighbor on the left. The area of the house is 400m.
- The expert was unable to inspect the property from the inside. The door was knocked, but there was no answer. Those present stated that they do not have keys to the house, as the beneficiary of the house is the first defendant and her children.
- The appraisal expert stated that he could evaluate the property through an external inspection, as there are no significant modifications to the property in question.
- The appraisal expert accompanying the inspection team examined the property from the outside in preparation for estimating its value according to real estate market prices.

Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall start at a base price of 267,300 KWD (Two hundred sixty-seven thousand, three hundred Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). To participate in the auction, a deposit of at least one-fifth of this price is required, either by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is accepted by the judge must deposit the full accepted price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was accepted does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction award will be confirmed in their favor, unless another person comes forward in this session offering to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at their liability based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 KWD, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures. The Clerk's Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bears no liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in their favor for a similar rent."

President of the Court of First Instance

# وزارة العدل
## إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق

### كشف بأسماء المتخلفين عن استلام شهادات إثبات الملكية

تعلن إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق بوزارة العدل عن وجود شهادات إثبات ملكية لم يستلمها أصحابها، وتدعوهم إلى الحضور إلى مقر الإدارة لاستلامها في أوقات الدوام الرسمي، وإلا فإن الإدارة ستضطر إلى إلغائها بعد مضي شهر من تاريخ هذا الإعلان.

# مرسوم أميري رقم ٥ لسنة ١٩٧٤
## بتعيين وزير العدل

- بعد الاطلاع على الدستور،
- وعلى الأمر الأميري الصادر بتاريخ ٨ ربيع الأول ١٣٩٤ هـ الموافق أول أبريل ١٩٧٤م،
- وبناء على عرض رئيس مجلس الوزراء،

**رسمنا بالآتي**

### مادة أولى
يعين السيد/ محمد أحمد الحمد وزيراً للعدل.

### مادة ثانية
على رئيس مجلس الوزراء تنفيذ هذا المرسوم، ويعمل به من تاريخ صدوره، وينشر في الجريدة الرسمية.

**أمير الكويت**
**صباح السالم الصباح**

**رئيس مجلس الوزراء**
**جابر الأحمد الجابر**

صدر بقصر السيف في: ٢ جمادى الأولى ١٣٩٤ هـ
الموافق: ٢٦ مايو ١٩٧٤ م

# Amiri Decree <orig>مرسوم أميري</orig> No. 5 of 1974
## Appointing the Minister of Justice <orig>وزير العدل</orig>

- After reviewing the Constitution,
- And the Amiri Order issued on 8 Rabi' al-Awwal 1394 H, corresponding to April 1, 1974,
- And upon the proposal of the Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig>,

**We decree the following**

### Article One
Mr. Mohammed Ahmed Al-Hamad <orig>محمد أحمد الحمد</orig> is appointed Minister of Justice <orig>وزيراً للعدل</orig>.

### Article Two
The Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig> shall implement this decree, and it shall come into force from the date of its issuance and be published in the Official Gazette.

**Amir of Kuwait <orig>أمير الكويت</orig>**
**Sabah Al-Salem Al-Sabah <orig>صباح السالم الصباح</orig>**

**Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig>**
**Jaber Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber <orig>جابر الأحمد الجابر</orig>**

Issued at Seif Palace on: 2 Jumada al-Awwal 1394 H
Corresponding to: May 26, 1974

## Description of the Thirteenth Property (According to the attached Description Certificate)
Property of Document No. 2284/2023 located in the Al-Jabriya <orig>الجابرية</orig> area – Plot (51), Block No. (1 A), Plan M/30777 – with an area of 1000 m2, to be sold at public auction with a base price of 1,750,000 K.D. (one million, seven hundred and fifty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
The property is an investment residence consisting of (ground floor + 5 typical floors + roof + carpenter's room). There are violations, namely: 1- An office was added on the ground floor. 2- An apartment was added on the fifth floor. 3- The balconies were enclosed.
** And according to the expert's report:
The disputed property is an old building located on a corner on an internal street No. (7), with an area of 1000 m2 as established by Document No. 2300/2023, bearing building number 22. Opposite it is a dirt lot overlooking the Fourth Ring Road (used as parking for the building's tenants). It consists of a mezzanine ground floor, five (5) typical floors, and a roof. There is an elevator and parking spaces. Its exterior is clad in marble, and it has a structurally separate shop on the ground floor named Black Moon Men's Salon.
- The plaintiff stated that the property is fully leased and he cannot enable the expert to inspect the apartments, and he stated that the components of the property in question are as follows:
i. The mezzanine ground floor has two (2) identical apartments in terms of components, each consisting of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
ii. The first and second floors are identical, and each floor consists of four (4) identical apartments in terms of components, each consisting of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
iii. The third floor consists of two (2) identical apartments in terms of components, each consisting of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen, and two (2) identical apartments in terms of components, each consisting of two rooms, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
iv. The fourth and fifth floors are identical, and each floor consists of four (4) identical apartments in terms of components, each consisting of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
The plaintiff's representative stated that the disputed property has central air conditioning, and that the monthly rent for each apartment ranges between 200 K.D. and 350 K.D., and the rent for the Black Moon Men's Salon is 1000 K.D. per month.

(one million, six hundred and fifty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

** And according to the expert's report:
The disputed property is an old building located on a corner on an internal street No. (7), with an area of 1000 m2 as established by Document No. 2300/2023, bearing building number 22. Opposite it is a dirt lot overlooking the Fourth Ring Road (used as parking). It consists of a mezzanine ground floor, five (5) typical floors, and a roof. There is an elevator and parking spaces. Its exterior is clad in marble, and it has a structurally separate shop on the ground floor named Exotic Car Rental.
- The plaintiff stated that the property is fully leased and he cannot enable the expert to inspect the apartments, and he stated that the components of the property in question are as follows:
a- The mezzanine ground floor has two (2) identical apartments in terms of components, each consisting of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
aa- The first and second floors are identical, and each floor consists of four (4) identical apartments in terms of components, each consisting of one room, a living room, a bathroom, and a kitchen.

## Description of the Thirteenth Property (According to the attached Description Certificate)
Property of Document No. 2292/2023 located in the Al-Jabriya <orig>الجابرية</orig> area – Plot (5), Block No. (5), Plan M/31742/A – with an area of 750 m2, to be sold at public auction with a base price of 860,000 K.D. (eight hundred and sixty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
The property is within a private residential area, consisting of a ground floor and a first floor.
** And according to the expert's report:
The disputed property is a private residential house of medium construction, located on two streets, front and back, and an alley (Street No. 14 and the main Abdullah Ali Dashti <orig>عبد الله علي دشتي</orig> Street). It consists of a ground floor, first floor, and roof. It has a yard surrounding the house, a garden, and a setback overlooking Abdullah Ali Dashti <orig>عبد الله علي دشتي</orig> Street. Its area is 750 m2 as established by Document No. 2292/2023, and the property has two (2) main entrances.
The ground floor consists of three (3) interconnected halls, an office room with its bathroom, a bathroom with washbasins, a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig>, a kitchen, and a servant's room with its bathroom.
The first floor has a living room, two (2) master bedrooms with their bathrooms, two (2) bedrooms, a bathroom, and a kitchenette.
The roof has the air conditioning units.
Property finishes: The floors are marble, the doors are wood, the lighting is pendant and spotlights, the walls are standard paint, the air conditioning is central, and the ceilings have gypsum decor.

### Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction begins at the base price, and participation in the auction requires payment of one-fifth of that

<header>
Kuwait Today Issue 1733 Seventy-First Year
67
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 H - 6/4/2025 G
</header>


Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction will be immediately reopened at their liability based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder will be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to execute a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."

President of the Court of First Instance

The property of Document No. 2971/2006, located in the Salmiya <orig>السالمية</orig> area - Plot (343) currently, previously 18, Block No. (10) currently, previously 222 - Plan M/39666, previously M/19523 - with an area of 863 m², to be sold at public auction with a starting price of 9,060,000 K.D. (Nine million and sixty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** And according to the description certificate:
- The property is in violation, consisting of several separate buildings made of light materials that do not conform to the architectural plan attached to the technical file.
** And according to the expert's report:
The disputed property, located in the Salmiya <orig>السالمية</orig> area, Block 10, Oman Street, as well as Al-Adasani Street, Avenue 1, was inspected as follows:
- The disputed property is a private hospital overlooking two streets. Its exterior cladding is made of aluminum composite panels (Alucobond). The disputed property has six electric elevators and three staircases, as well as five entrances. The air conditioning in the disputed property is central, with unit-based systems in some parts.
- The disputed property is currently unoccupied and consists of three buildings that are connected on the ground floor and separate on the other (upper) floors, where it is not possible to move between the three separate buildings except through the common ground floor.
- The common ground floor consists of a patient reception area, a pharmacy, a radiology department with five rooms, an analysis laboratory with four rooms, an insurance office, and two rooms for medical waste

# Announcement of a Property Sale by Public Auction

The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale by public auction of the property described below on Monday, 5/5/2025 - Hall 48 - on the second floor of the Justice Palace at 9:00 AM - in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 183/2023 Sales/1 and its related cases.

Filed by:
Kuwait International Bank <orig>بنك الكويت الدولي</orig>.

Against:
1- Al-Rashed Hospital Company - Abdullah Rashed Al-Saif & Partners <orig>شركة مستشفى الراشد- عبدالله راشد السيف وشركاه</orig>.

a- Thaer Abdullah Rashed Al-Saif <orig>ثائر عبدالله راشد السيف</orig>.
b- Feryal Abdulrahim Omar <orig>فريال عبدالرحيم عمر</orig>.
c- Nael Abdullah Al-Rashed Al-Saif <orig>نائل عبدالله الراشد السيف</orig>.
d- Saif Al-Din Abdullah Rashed Al-Saif <orig>سيف الدين عبدالله راشد السيف</orig>.
3- Ahli United Bank <orig>البنك الأهلي المتحد</orig>.
In Case No.: 3/2025 Sales 1
Automated No. 250008590

. The first building consists of three floors as detailed below:
The first floor consists of a maternity ward and a nursery for children.
The second floor consists of operating rooms.
The third floor consists of a central maintenance room, an in-vitro fertilization (IVF) department, and a doctors' lounge.
The second building consists of five floors, each floor containing seven rooms, which are post-operative rooms.
. The third building consists of two floors as detailed below:
The first floor consists of twelve rooms for surgery clinics, three rooms for ophthalmology clinics, one room for an ear, nose, and throat (ENT) clinic, three rooms for a urology clinic, two rooms for an internal medicine clinic, one room for nutrition, two rooms for a dermatology clinic, and a computer (server) room.
The second floor consists of ten rooms for cosmetic clinics and four rooms for administration.
. The representative of the plaintiff company identified Plot No. 18, mentioned in Real Estate Document No. 2971/2006, and it was found that the current plot number is 22218 and the automated number is 90257757 according to the Kuwait Finder program. It is a vacant plot of land with only two Kirby buildings constructed on it.
. The representative of the plaintiff company identified Plot No. 14, mentioned in Real Estate Document No. 2971/2006, and it was found that the current plot number is 22214 and the automated number is 96289741 according to the Kuwait Finder program. It is a vacant plot of land only.
The representative of the plaintiff company stated that a part of the disputed property (the hospital) described above (reception – dental clinics – aviation medicine room – maintenance room – nursing room – the two shops – in addition to the third building) is located within Plot No. 21 (346) (currently), automated number 90257781 according to the Kuwait Finder program, is not part of the lawsuit, as that plot belongs to State Properties and is not owned by the defendants. The expert notes the presence of a sticker that reads "State Properties" during the inspection.
. The expert notes the existence of a shop used as a laundry, belonging to the second building, specifically on the ground floor, bearing the name "Oti Clean Laundry," which is for sale.
The representative of the plaintiff company stated that the lawsuit pertains to properties No. (14 - 18), which are vacant plots as described above, and properties No. (19 - 20), which are part of the building (the hospital) described above, and not the entire building.
Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, at the time the sale session is held, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their expense during the same session, based on the price at which the sale had been awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction will be reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction shall be immediately reopened at their expense on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease agreement in their favor for a similar rent."
President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

## Property Description (According to the attached Description Certificate)
The property of Document No. 7146/1995, located in the Jaber Al-Ali <orig>جابر العلي</orig> area - Plot (94), Block No. (4), Plan M/36969, with an area of 393.6 m², to be sold at public auction for a base price of KWD 260,000 (Two hundred and sixty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

** And according to what is stated in the Description Certificate:
The property has the following violations:
1. Unlicensed construction on the ground floor with an area of 25 m².
2. Unlicensed construction on the first floor with an area of 65 m².
3. There is an adjoining structure on the side of the yard and the side passage.
4. There is an external staircase.

** And according to what is stated in the Description Certificate:
The property subject of the dispute, located in the Jaber Al-Ali <orig>جابر العلي</orig> area - Block 4 - Street 33 - Plan M/36874, with an area of 301 m², to be sold at public auction for a base price of KWD 300,000 (Three hundred thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

** And according to what is stated in the Description Certificate:
- No violations exist.

** And according to what is stated in the expert's report:
The disputed property located in the Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area - Block 2 - Street 1 - Jada - House 3, automated address number 12821201, at the time of inspection is as follows:
1. The disputed property conforms in terms of general and special specifications and boundaries to Document No. 4297/1993, with an area of 301 m².
2. The disputed property is a private residence house overlooking two streets (a corner plot), Street No. (1) and Jada No. (8).
3. The disputed property consists of a ground floor and a first floor, detailed as follows:
    a- The ground floor consists of 2 rooms + bathroom + living room + kitchen + an external diwaniya with a bathroom.
    b- The first floor consists of 5 rooms + 3 bathrooms + living room.
4. The exterior cladding is limestone.
5. The house's air conditioning is split units.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction begins at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at his expense in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at his expense based on the price that was awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1. This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2. The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3. The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in his favor for a comparable rent."

President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

3- Nadia Marzouq Nay Saad Al-Watri <orig>نادية مرزوق ناي سعد الوطري</orig>.

Versus:
1- Aida Fallah Fahad Al-Watri <orig>عيدة فلاح فهد الوطري</orig>.
2- Saad Marzouq Nay Saad Al-Watri <orig>سعد مرزوق ناي سعد الوطري</orig>.

Property Description: (According to the attached description certificate)
The property of Document No. 468/1981 located in the Al-Rabiya <orig>الرابية</orig> area – Plot (136), Block No. (4), Plan M/27344 – with a total area of 1000 m2, to be sold at public auction with a starting price of KWD 800,000 / Eight hundred thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>.
** And according to what is stated in the description certificate:
- The violation on the property is an increase in the building ratio on the roof, estimated at 25 m2 (room + bathroom).
** And according to what is stated in the expert's report:
The first subject of dispute and its physical inspection is located in Al-Rabiya <orig>الرابية</orig>, Block 4, Street (7), House (9), Plot (136), and the automated number is (11810199).
The inspection was carried out as follows:
The subject of dispute is a private residence overlooking an internal street, a side alley, and a back alley, and is bordered by one neighbor. The exterior facade is stone, and the air conditioning is central. According to the property certificate, the document number is (468/1981) and its area is 1000 square meters.
It has an elevator and one main entrance. The subject of dispute consists of three floors: ground floor, first floor, second floor, a basement, and a roof, detailed as follows:
Ground Floor: Consists of (3) halls, (3) rooms, and (3) bathrooms. There is an external Diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> shared with the adjacent plot, an external kitchen, and an external room for servants.
First Floor: Consists of (8) rooms, (4) bathrooms, a hall, and a balcony.
Second Floor: Consists of two apartments, each apartment comprising (3) rooms and (2) bathrooms.
Roof: A maid's room and water heater machinery.
Basement: Used as a storage for children's toys and consists of a hall and a storeroom.

House 12, with automated number 14062376, was inspected as follows:
- The property subject of the lawsuit is located on a street, an alley, and a parking area for the cooperative society branch. Its exterior cladding is limestone, and its area is 393.60 m2.
- The property consists of a ground floor, a first floor, a roof, and two annexes. The first annex consists of a Diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig>, a bathroom, washbasins, a storeroom, and a room. Above the first annex is an apartment consisting of a hall, a room, a bathroom, and a kitchen, with the apartment's entrance from inside the property. The second annex consists of two floors, each floor having an apartment consisting of two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
The ground floor of the property consists of two halls and a kitchen with two entrances, one from inside the property and the other from the outside. The first floor consists of two apartments; the first apartment consists of a hall, two rooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen, while the second apartment consists of two rooms and a bathroom.

Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction begins at the starting price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at their liability on the basis of the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease contract in their favor for a similar rent."

President of the Court of First Instance

# Announcement of Public Auction for the Sale of a Property
The Clerk's Department <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the Court of First Instance <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 5/1/2025 – Hall 52 – on the second floor of the Justice Palace at 9:00 AM – in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 486/2024 Sales/3
Filed by: Intisar Haji Ali Sirali <orig>انتصار حاجي على سيرالي</orig>.
Against:
1- Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Qailani <orig>عبدالله على عبدالله القيلاني</orig>.
2- The Director of the Real Estate Registration and Authentication Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig>, in his capacity.
3- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.
Property Description: According to the attached description certificate.
Property under Title Deed No. 17425/1995 located in Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig>, Block 2, Plot No. (7), Parcel No. (5) of Plan No. M/36953, with an area of 400 m2.
* Violations exist:
1- Installation of an unlicensed elevator.
2- There are lightweight Kirby materials on the first floor on the street-facing side of the property, which violates the plan.
* Inspection:
The disputed property is located in the Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig> area – Parcel 5 – Street 7 – Plot No. 7 – House No. 35, PACI No.: 132699818. The inspection was conducted as follows:
The disputed property has an area of 400 square meters, according to Title Deed No. 17425/1995 submitted in the plaintiff's document portfolio during the session of 1/16/2024, document No. 2.
The disputed property is a private residence of average construction, with front and back access, two entrances, and is bordered by neighbors on two sides.
The disputed property consists of a ground floor and a first floor.
At the time of inspection, it was found that a second floor, a half third floor, and an elevator room with a single entrance from the side of the house have been added. These additions are in the structural frame (black skeleton) phase.
The ground floor consists of a hall with washbasins and a bathroom, another hall with washbasins and a bathroom, a master bedroom with a bathroom, a main kitchen, and a servant's room with a bathroom.
The first floor consists of a hall with a balcony, a kitchenette, a master bedroom with a bathroom separated by a door. The right side consists of two rooms and a bathroom, and the left side consists of a master bedroom with a bathroom and another room.
The exterior cladding is rough-faced Jordanian stone.
Air conditioning: The ground floor halls have central AC, while the rest of the floor and the first floor have split units.
Flooring: One hall on the ground floor has marble flooring; the rest of the property's floors are ceramic.
The Expert Appraiser <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> inspected the property and stated that he is able to estimate the property's value and determine its base price in preparation for its sale by public auction and to submit a report thereon.
## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction will start at a base price of 370,000 K.D. (Three Hundred Seventy Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of this price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale had been awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction shall be reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the ten percent increase, the auction shall be immediately reopened at their liability, based on the price at which it was previously awarded to them. In this session, no bid shall be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.

# Announcement of Real Estate Sale by Public Auction
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale by public auction of the property described below, to be held on Thursday, 5/1/2025, in Hall 52 on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig> at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 2023/536 Sales/3.
Filed by: Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
Against:
First: The heirs of the deceased Rakhees Nasser Hadi Al-Dhafiri <orig>رخيص ناصر هادي الضفيري</orig> and the deceased Manara Marzouq Yaqoub Al-Dhafiri <orig>مناره مرزوق يعقوب الضفيري</orig>, who are:
1- Ali Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>عالي رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
2- Bader Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>بدر رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
3- Bandar Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>بندر رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
4- Oudah Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>عوده رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
5- Tarqiyah Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>طرقيه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
6- Latifa Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>لطيفه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
7- Fatma Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>فطمه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
8- Khazna Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>خزنه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
9- Noura Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>نوره رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
Second: The heirs of the deceased Badriya Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>بدريه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
- Talal Hatem Al-Dhafiri <orig>طلال حاتم الضفيري</orig>, in his capacity as the natural guardian of his children (Bandar, Abdulaziz, Fatima).
Third: Director General of the Public Authority for Housing Welfare <orig>مدير عام المؤسسة العامه للرعاية السكنية</orig>, in his capacity.
Fourth: Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وكيل وزارة العدل</orig> – Real Estate Registration and Authentication Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig>, in his capacity.
Fifth: Legal Representative of Kuwait Municipality <orig>الممثل القانوني لبلدية الكويت</orig>, in his capacity.
First: Property Description: According to the attached certificate of description.
- Property under Document No. 1995/783 located in Al-Jahra <orig>الجهراء</orig> – Al-Naseem <orig>النسيم</orig> – Plot No. (256) – Block (1) of Plan No. (M/37003), with an area of (400 m²).
Note:
Violation report No. 25622 was issued on 8/1/2023, for an unlicensed structure on the ground floor + a Kirby roof.
*Inspection:
On 4/12/2023, we proceeded to the Al-Jahra <orig>الجهراء</orig> area – Al-Naseem <orig>النسيم</orig> – Block 1 – Street 28 – Plot No. 256, House No. 21, in the presence and under the guidance of the plaintiff in person. The defendants or their representatives were absent. The Appointed Expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig>, Mr. Saad Al-Daihani <orig>سعد الديحاني</orig>, was present, and the inspection was conducted as follows:
- The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is a plot located at the aforementioned address, consisting of a ground floor and a first floor. The property has front and back access and is clad on the exterior with beige lime plaster.
- The expert was unable to inspect the property from the inside after knocking on the door and receiving no answer. The expert noted that the main door was secured with an external lock.
The Appointed Expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig>, Mr. Saad Al-Daihani <orig>سعد الديحاني</orig>, inspected the disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> and took all necessary notes in preparation for estimating its value.
- The expert determined that the area of the property is 400 m².
Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction will start at a base price of 186,988.500 KWD (one hundred eighty-six thousand, nine hundred eighty-eight Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and five hundred fils). To participate in the auction, a deposit of at least one-fifth of this price must be paid by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose bid was approved fails to deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be repeated at his liability during the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, a judgment awarding the auction to him shall be issued, unless another person comes forward in that session offering to purchase with an increase of one-tenth, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction shall be repeated in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the one-tenth increase, the auction shall be immediately repeated at his liability, based on the price that was awarded to him in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 KWD, lawyer's fees, expert's fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in accordance with the law. Those initiating the sale procedures do so at their own responsibility, and the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> shall bear no liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property with an inspection that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the official gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states: "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to issue a lease contract in his favor for a rent equivalent to that of similar properties."
President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

# Announcement of Real Estate Sale by Public Auction
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the sale by public auction of the property described below, to be held on Monday, 5/5/2025, in Hall 48 on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig> at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 2022/636 Sales/1.
Filed by: Abdullah Ali Jassim <orig>عبدالله علي جاسم</orig>.
Against:
1- Mohammed Abdullah Ali Jassim <orig>محمد عبدالله علي جاسم</orig>.
2- Jassim Abdullah Ali Jassim <orig>جاسم عبدالله علي جاسم</orig>.
3- Numaira Abdullah Ali Jassim <orig>نميره عبدالله علي جاسم</orig>.
4- Sakina Abdullah Ali Jassim <orig>سكينه عبدالله علي جاسم</orig>.

7- Director General of the Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>مدير عام بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>, in his capacity.
Property Description: (According to the attached certificate of description)
Property under Document No. 2011/8983 located in the Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> area – Plot No. 20 – Block No. 11, Western Part – Plan M/36888, with an area of 300.125 m², to be sold by public auction at a starting price of 295,000 KWD (two hundred ninety-five thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

<header>
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 H - 2025/4/6 G
73
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-first Year
</header>

** According to the property description certificate:
- The property is a private residence consisting of a ground floor + first floor, and there is a violation, which is a structure built of light materials.

** According to the expert's report:
In the session of 6/6/2022, the expert went to the Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> area, Block 11, Plot 20, in the presence of the knowledge expert Mr. Saad Al-Daihani <orig>سعد الديحاني</orig> and with the guidance and access provided by the third and fourth defendants. The plaintiff was absent despite being notified of the session date, as were the rest of the defendants. The expert notes a discrepancy in the street, avenue, and house numbers from what is stated in the statement of claim, as the inspection confirmed that the street number is 1, the avenue is 3, and the house is 27.
The disputed property is located on a single internal street, surrounded by neighbors on both sides, and its rear overlooks the main street No. 207, named after Mohammed bin Hamada Al-Ajmi <orig>محمد بن حمادة العجمي</orig>.
The disputed property is an old government house consisting of a ground floor, first floor, and a roof. It is clad in pink "sigma" paint, has two entrances (front and rear), and the rear setback is an independent garden and parking area.
The third defendant enabled the expert to enter and inspect the property, where the following was found:
- The ground floor consists of a small courtyard overlooked by a diwaniya with a bathroom and washbasins, a driver's room with its entrance from Street No. 1, a kitchen, two bathrooms, two halls, and a storage area under the stairs.
- The first floor consists of two apartments. The first consists of a master bedroom, a small hall, another room, and a bathroom. The second apartment consists of 3 bedrooms, two bathrooms, and a kitchen.
- The roof contains a master bedroom.
- The property's finishes are as follows: ceramic floors, regular paint on the walls, lighting is spotlights and pendants, and the air conditioning is split units.
The expert and the knowledge expert inspected the property externally and internally. The knowledge expert also reviewed the property deed No. 8983, which states that the area of the disputed plot is 300.125 m², and also reviewed the sketch plan of the property previously submitted by the plaintiff's agent, in preparation for taking the necessary steps to estimate the property's value according to the market price.

- Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction begins at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is accepted by the judge must deposit the full accepted price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
Third: If the person whose bid was accepted does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale had been awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction award will be confirmed in their favor, unless another person comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with the ten percent increase, the auction is immediately reopened at their liability based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder will be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures. The Court Clerk's Department <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> at the Court of First Instance bears no liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement is published in the official gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedure Law.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedure Law.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedure Law states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to issue a lease contract in their favor for a rent equivalent to the market rate."

President of the Court of First Instance

# Announcement of Public Auction for a Property
The Court Clerk's Department <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> at the Court of First Instance announces the public auction of the property described below on Monday, 5/5/2025, in Hall 48 on the second floor of the Justice Palace at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 2022/642 Sales/1.
Filed by: Fatima Abdullah Mardhi Al-Rashidi <orig>فاطمة عبدالله مرضى الرشيدي</orig>.
Against:
1- Hussein Abdullah Mardhi Al-Rashidi <orig>حسين عبدالله مرضى الرشيدي</orig>.
2- The Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice for Real Estate Registration and Notarization Affairs <orig>وكيل وزارة العدل لشئون التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig>, in his capacity.
3- The Director of the Execution Department <orig>مدير إدارة التنفيذ</orig>, in his capacity.
Property Description: (According to the attached property description certificate)
The property under Deed No. 2022/3834, located in the Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area – Plot No. 327 – Block No. 5 – Plan M/36874, with an area of 301 m², will be sold at public auction with a base price of 230,000 K.D. (Two hundred and thirty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the property description certificate:
The property is a private residence consisting of a ground floor + first floor + roof, and it has violations regarding an increase in the building percentage on the roof on the side of the alleyway, and the roof is made of Kirby material, report No. 14406.

** According to the expert's report:
- The disputed property, located in the Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area, Block (5), Street (1), Avenue (6), Plot (327), House (26), with an area of 301 m², was inspected as follows:
- The disputed property is a private residence with an area of (301 square meters) according to Deed No. (3834). The property consists of a ground floor, first floor, and a roof. It is located on one street and an alleyway with a transformer. The exterior is clad in stone. It is adjacent to a neighbor on the right side, and on the other side, there is an alleyway with an electrical transformer.
- The expert knocked on the door, but no one answered.
- During the inspection, the expert found that the disputed property is adjacent to another property from the rear, separated by a wall. The expert took photographs and will attach them.

the first and second floors, and there is an increase in the building area, which is in violation of the regulations and bylaws of the Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>.

***Inspection:***
On 3/8/2023, we proceeded to inspect the property subject of the lawsuit, located in the Qortuba <orig>قرطبة</orig> area, Block (2), Street (3), Avenue (4), House (38), with automated number (90482719). This was done in the presence and under the guidance of the plaintiff's agent and the first defendant, and in the presence of the Expert Witness, Mr. Osama Al-Ruwaih <orig>أسامة الرويح</orig>. The inspection was carried out as follows: –
- The disputed property is a residential plot consisting of a basement, ground floor, first floor, and a roof, clad in Jordanian stone, and is located on two streets (a corner plot).
- The disputed property conforms to Document No. 2022/683 and has an area of 587.5 square meters.
- The first defendant indicated the components of the property as follows:
1- The basement consists of a hall + 2 bedrooms + a bathroom + an office room.
2- The ground floor consists of a hall and a salon + a bathroom + a refrigerator storage room + a main kitchen + a driver's room with a bathroom in the yard and a diwaniya with a bathroom.
3- The first mezzanine consists of 3 bedrooms + two bathrooms.
4- The first floor consists of a hall + a bedroom + a bathroom + a kitchen.
5- The second mezzanine consists of 4 bedrooms + a bathroom.
6- The roof consists of two bedrooms for domestic workers + a bathroom + a storage room.
7- Central air conditioning.

## Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin with a base price of KWD 720,000 (seven hundred and twenty thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). To participate in the auction, a deposit of at least one-fifth of this price must be paid by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Execution Department at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, he must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction shall be repeated at his own risk during the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, a judgment awarding the auction shall be issued in his favor, unless another person comes forward in this session who agrees to purchase with an increase of one-tenth, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction shall be repeated in the same session on the basis of this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with an increase of one-tenth, the auction shall be immediately repeated at his own risk based on the price at which it was previously awarded to him. In this session, no bid shall be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for the transfer and registration of ownership, the execution procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those initiating the sale procedures and at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure states that "If the person whose property has been expropriated is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to execute a lease agreement in his favor for a fair market rent."

**President of the Court of First Instance <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>**

Filed by: Abdullah Nasser Abdullah Al-Saqabi <orig>عبدالله ناصر عبدالله الصقعبي</orig>

The expert review, upon comparing the plans submitted by the two plaintiffs, revealed minor changes to the disputed property in the form of an expansion, where a room was added to each apartment on the first and second floors, and that the rest of the property's components conform to the plans.
The flooring in the property was changed on the ground floor to marble ceramic and ceramic on the upper floors. The air conditioning is central, and there is no elevator in the property.
The second defendant, Faisal <orig>فيصل</orig>, stated that the beneficiaries of the property are as follows: on the ground floor is the defendant Sheikha <orig>شيخه</orig>; on the first floor is the defendant Khalid <orig>خالد</orig> and his family in the apartment, and in the suite is the defendant Abeer <orig>عبير</orig>; on the second floor is the defendant Faisal <orig>فيصل</orig> and his family, their brother Hussein <orig>حسين</orig>, and the defendant Munira <orig>منيرة</orig>. He stated that the two plaintiffs do not reside in the property.
Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall begin with a base price of KWD 324,000 (three hundred twenty-four thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate at the Ministry of Justice <orig>إدارة التنفيذ بوزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit, during the sale session, the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees.
Third: If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their liability in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session who agrees to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction is reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction will be immediately reopened at their liability based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: The successful bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those initiating the sale procedures, and at their own responsibility, without the Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The judgment awarding the auction is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Civil and Commercial Procedures Law <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draft a lease agreement in their favor for a comparable rent."
President of the Court of First Instance
