# Announcement of Public Auction for a Property
The Clerks' Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below on Thursday, 1/5/2025, in Hall 52 on the second floor of the Justice Palace at 9:00 AM. This is in execution of the court judgment issued in Case No. 741/2023 Sales/3.

**Filed by:**
1- Shurouq Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>شروق عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
2- Mai Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>مي عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.

**Against:**
1- Sheikha Fahad Saqr <orig>شيخة فهد صقر</orig>.
2- Faisal Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>فيصل عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
3- Khalid Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>خالد عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
4- Munira Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>منيرة عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
5- Abeer Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>عبير عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
6- Masha'el Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>مشاعل عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
7- Nouf Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>نوف عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
8- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>

**First: Property Description:** According to the attached description certificate.
Property under Document No. 9308/1995, located in Jaber Al-Ali <orig>جابر العلي</orig> – Plot 74 <orig>قسيمة ٧٤</orig> – Block 1 <orig>قطعة ١</orig> – from Plan No. M/36966 – with an area of 392 m2.
*Note:
There is a major violation on the roof.

*Inspection:
The expert team visited the disputed property on 18/9/2023, located in the Jaber Al-Ali <orig>جابر العلي</orig> suburb area, Block 1, Street 3, House 7, Plot 74, with an area of 392 square meters. The visit was conducted in the presence and under the guidance of the plaintiffs' agent, the second defendant Faisal Al-Hajri <orig>فيصل الهاجري</orig>, and Mr. Osama Al-Ruwaih <orig>أسامة الرويح</orig>, the appointed expert, as shown in (Appendix 1 - Inspection Report No. (8)). The inspection was carried out as follows:
* The disputed property is a house located on a single street with a yellow-orange limestone facade. It has two entrances from the street, one for the Diwaniya <orig>الديوانية</orig> and the other for the house courtyard. The property is relatively old.
* The second defendant, Faisal <orig>فيصل</orig>, allowed the expert team to enter and inspect the property, and the inspection was carried out as follows:
* The ground floor consists of a reception hall, a bathroom, a bedroom, a living room, a staircase, a main kitchen, a dining room, and a bathroom. Externally, there is a Diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with washbasins and a bathroom.
* The first floor consists of a suite with 2 rooms and 2 bathrooms, and an apartment with 3 rooms, 2 bathrooms, and a hall.
* The second floor, according to the defendant's statement, is identical to the first floor. The expert team was unable to inspect it due to the family's presence; however, the plans submitted to the expert team show that it is identical to the first floor.
* The roof level: It has a Kirby-style structure consisting of a room and a bathroom for the domestic workers.

## Filed by:
1- Afrah Hamad Abdulsayyed Al-Shatti <orig>افراح حمد عبدالسيد الشطي</orig>, on her own behalf and in her capacity as custodian and guardian of her son, Abdulrahman Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>عبدالرحمن راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
2- Yousef Rashed Othman Abdullah Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>يوسف راشد عثمان عبدالله عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
3- Fiddah Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>فضة راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
4- Moudhi Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>موضى راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.

## Against:
1- Aisha Salem Abdullah Bughaith <orig>عائشة سالم عبدالله بوغيث</orig>.
2- Rasha Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>رشا راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
3- Rana Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>رنا راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
4- Bodour Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>بدور راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
5- Abdullah Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>عبدالله راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
6- Othman Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>عثمان راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
7- Hamad Rashed Othman Al-Shaqeehi <orig>حمد راشد عثمان الشقيحي</orig>.
8- Director of the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>مدير إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig>, in his capacity.
9- Zahra Khidr Ali Al-Fares <orig>زهرة خضر علي الفارس</orig>.

### First: Property Description: According to the attached description certificate.
- The property under Document No. (14237/1997) located in Sabah Al-Salem Suburb <orig>ضاحية صباح السالم</orig> – Block No. (8), Plot No. (2) of Plan No. (M/36984), with an area of (300.325 m2), taking into account the right of residence for the divorcée, Zahra Khidr Ali Al-Fares <orig>زهرة خضر على الفارس</orig>, until the end of the children's custody period, in accordance with the letter from the Real Estate Registration Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري</orig>.

**Note:**
There is a violation, which is a room built on the roof, according to the Municipality's letter.

***Inspection:***
- The property is located in the Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> area – Block 8 – Street 1 – Avenue 15 – House – Plot 2, Automated No. 11942204, where the inspection was conducted as follows:
- The disputed property is a government house located on two streets (front and back), an internal street and a main street, bordered by two neighbors, and consists of a ground floor, a first floor, and a roof.
- The property has an area of 300 m2 according to the document submitted by the plaintiffs' agent in the session of 13/1/2022. The exterior is coated with Sigma paint, and the air conditioning is central and split-unit.
- The disputed property has two entrances. The first is on the internal street side and is used exclusively by the plaintiffs. It consists of a portion of the ground floor, which includes a diwaniya + bathroom and washbasins + four (4) rooms + three (3) bathrooms + a living room + a kitchen.
- As for the second entrance on the main street side, the door was knocked on several times, but no one answered. The plaintiffs' agent stated that this part is used exclusively by the defendant and Ms. Zahra Khidr Al-Fares <orig>زهراء خضر الفارس</orig> (the decedent's ex-wife and mother of the second to seventh defendants). Therefore, he is unable to grant the expert access to inspect this part, explaining that it consists of: a kitchen on the ground floor, the entire first floor, and the roof.

### Second: Auction Conditions:
**First:** The auction shall start at a base price of KWD 317,115/- (Three hundred seventeen thousand, one hundred and fifteen Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). To participate in the auction, a payment of at least one-fifth of this price is required by a certified check from the drawee bank or a letter of guarantee from a bank in favor of the Enforcement Directorate <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
**Second:** The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees during the sale session.
**Third:** If the person whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the auction will be reopened at their expense in the same session, based on the price at which the sale was awarded.
**Fourth:** If the bidder deposits the price in the following session, the auction award will be confirmed in their favor, unless another person comes forward in that session offering to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the auction will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
**Fifth:** If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the following session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the auction will be immediately reopened at their expense based on the price that was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid will be considered unless it is accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder will be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
**Sixth:** The winning bidder shall, in all cases, bear the fees for title transfer and registration, the enforcement procedure expenses amounting to KWD 200, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
**Seventh:** This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request and responsibility of those initiating the sale procedures, without the Clerk's Department of the Court of First Instance <orig>إدارة الكتاب بالمحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
**Eighth:** The winning bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Notice:
1- This sale announcement is published in the Official Gazette in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil and Commercial Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose property was expropriated is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the winning bidder is obligated to issue a lease contract in their favor for a similar rent."

President of the Court of First Instance

# Ministry of Finance
## Announcement of Sale by Sealed-Bid Auction
### Auction No. (2456) and Auction No. (2457)
The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> announces the sale of medical beds, office furniture, steel cabinets, lighting fixtures, heaters, wheelchairs, air conditioning ducts, wooden doors, air conditioning units, a steel structure (cold room), an emergency generator, a pile of wood, a pile of air conditioning ducts, empty fire extinguishers, a pile of iron, elevators and their accessories, electrical panels, signboards, a pile of steel, lighting, gas cylinders, and small barrels by sealed-bid auction at the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> according to the following details: -
1- **Location for receiving the terms and conditions booklet and submitting bids:** Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> - Financial Affairs - Central Archives and Files Section, from 6/4/2025 to 10/4/2025. The documents will be provided for a non-refundable fee of (50) Dinars, payable via K-Net at the Ministry of Health's cashier. Note that two separate documents will be sold:
    **A- Auction No. (2456):** Document for the sale of medical beds, office furniture, steel cabinets, lighting fixtures, heaters, wheelchairs, air conditioning ducts, wooden doors, air conditioning units, a steel structure (cold room).
    **B- Auction No. (2457):** Document for the sale of an emergency generator, a pile of wood, a pile of air conditioning ducts, empty fire extinguishers, a pile of iron, elevators and their accessories, electrical panels, signboards, a pile of steel, lighting, gas cylinders, and small barrels.
Upon receiving the terms and conditions booklet, the bidder will sign a declaration and undertaking to adhere to the specified deadline for submitting the bid to the Central Sales Committee at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.
2- **Inspection Date:** (5) working days from 6/4/2025 - 10/4/2025. Inspection Time: During official working hours.
3- Location for receiving those wishing to inspect the items for both auctions:
- Auction No. (2456): Al-Sabah Area <orig>منطقة الصباح</orig> (Psychiatric Medicine site).

- • Bids shall be submitted on Sunday, **04/13/2025**, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> – Block **12** – Third Floor – General Warehousing Affairs Department – Central Sales Section, according to the time specified for the bidder by the Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (No bid will be accepted after the specified time for the bidder has passed).

### Special Conditions for the Auction:
- The bidder must be a Kuwaiti – individual or company – registered in the Commercial Register and with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>. A foreigner may participate, provided they have a Kuwaiti partner or agent who is a merchant under a notarized contract. (Must attach: a copy of the Chamber of Commerce and Industry certificate, a copy of the company license, a copy of the Civil ID, and an authorization letter certified by the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, all of which must be valid).
- Kuwaiti individuals are permitted to participate in the auction (a copy of the Civil ID must be attached).
- To receive the bid book for bidders: Please contact Ms. Zainab Agha <orig>زينب أغا</orig>, Tel: **24622342**
- Site Inspection Officials:
  a - Auction No. (2456): Mr. Hamed Mesad Al-Dasbati <orig>حامد مسعد الدسبطي</orig>, Tel: **65868677**
  b - Auction No. (2457): Mr. Mohammed Hassan Attia <orig>محمد حسن عطية</orig>, Tel: **66344465**
- Central Sales Committee at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> / Tel: (**22481971**).
- Website address: **www.mof.gov.kw**

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Finance <orig>وكيل وزارة المالية</orig>

# Announcement
## Sale by Sealed-Bid Auction: Auction No. (2458) and Auction No. (2459)

The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> announces the sale of assorted iron and metals, lighting poles of various sizes, other materials, filters, furniture, steel, printing machines, computers and their accessories, equipment and insulators, chalets, batteries, iron reels, wooden reels, meters, and fire extinguishers by sealed-bid auction at the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>, according to the following details:

1- Location for receiving the bid book and participation offer for the auction: Warehouses Department – Subhan <orig>صبحان</orig> Warehouses, from **04/06/2025** to **04/10/2025**. The documents will be provided for a non-refundable fee of (300) Dinars, payable via K-Net (at the cashier of the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> – South Surra <orig>جنوب السرة</orig> – Accounts Department – Cashier Section, Ground Floor). Please note that two separate documents will be sold:
- a- Auction No. (2458): Document for the sale of assorted iron and metals, lighting poles of various sizes, and other materials.
- b- Auction No. (2459): Document for the sale of filters, furniture, steel, printing machines, computers and their accessories, equipment and insulators, chalets, batteries, iron reels, wooden reels, meters, and fire extinguishers.

At the time of receiving the bid book, the bidder will sign a declaration and undertaking to adhere to the specified appointment for submitting the bid to the Central Sales Committee at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.

2- Inspection Date: (5) working days from **04/13/2025**–**04/17/2025**
Inspection Time: From 8:00 AM to 1:00 PM.

3- Location for receiving those wishing to inspect for both auctions: Subhan <orig>صبحان</orig> Warehouses.

4- Date of bid submission and envelope opening:
- • Bids shall be submitted on Sunday, **04/20/2025**, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> – Block **12** – Third Floor – General Warehousing Affairs Department – Central Sales Section, according to the time specified for the bidder by the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig> (No bid will be accepted after the specified time for the bidder has passed).
- • Envelopes will be opened and the auction held on Monday, **04/21/2025**, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Ministries Complex <orig>مجمع الوزارات</orig> – Block **12** – Third Floor – General Warehousing Affairs Department.
- • The winning bidder will be announced on the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> website on Monday, **04/21/2025**.
- • Checks will be returned to unsuccessful bidders on Tuesday, **04/22/2025**.
- • Certified checks / bank guarantees shall be made out in the name of the Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy <orig>وزارة الكهرباء والماء والطاقة المتجددة</orig>.

### Special Conditions for Both Auctions:
1- The bidder must be a Kuwaiti establishment or company registered in the Commercial Register and with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>. A foreigner may participate, provided they have a Kuwaiti partner or agent who is a merchant under a notarized contract. (Must attach: a copy of the Chamber of Commerce and Industry certificate, a copy of the company license, and an authorization letter certified by the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, all of which must be valid).
2- Vehicles for loading materials are not permitted to leave the site until they have obtained a material exit permit from the members of the Material Removal Follow-up Committee, with no fewer than four members of the said committee present.
3- Bidders must sign the form prepared by the Warehouses Department, declaring and undertaking that they have inspected the materials subject to the auction in a manner that negates any lack of knowledge.

### Special Conditions for Auction (2459):
1- The winning bidder is obligated to provide the committee with proof of their commitment to send the batteries to recycling plants approved by the Environment Public Authority <orig>الهيئة العامة للبيئة</orig> within a maximum period of (60) days from the date of signing the contract.
2- Provide the committee with a customs declaration issued by the General Administration of Customs <orig>الإدارة العامة للجمارك</orig> stating that the batteries have been exported outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> within a maximum period of (60) days from the date of signing the contract.
- To receive the bid book and for the site inspection official for both auctions: Please contact Engineer Ali Al-Shammari <orig>علي الشمري</orig>, Tel: **99889495**.
- Central Sales Committee at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> / Tel: (**22481979**).
- Website address: **www.mof.gov.kw**

Undersecretary of the Ministry of Finance <orig>وكيل وزارة المالية</orig>

# Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig>
## Announcement
Re-issuance of Public Tender No. (DA/M/764) for Providing Cleaning Workers for Amiri Vehicles for the year 2025
The Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> announces the issuance of Public Tender No. (DA/M/764) for providing cleaning workers for Amiri vehicles for the year 2025. Companies or institutions specialized in this field who wish to participate may obtain the tender terms and documents during official working hours from (Amiri Diwan – Bayan Palace – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7 – Tenders and Follow-up Department). This is available during official working hours starting from the date of this announcement's publication in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) for a non-refundable fee of (75/- K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> (payment via K-Net only) for the booklet. Small and medium-sized enterprises are exempt from this fee (upon presentation of a certificate proving their status), starting from Sunday, 6/4/2025, from 8:30 AM to 1:00 PM, taking into account the following:
- The deadline for submitting bids is 1:30 PM on Thursday, 17/4/2025. No bids will be accepted after this time.
- Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Tenders and Follow-up Department – Bayan Palace – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7.
- A preliminary bid bond of not less than (2%) must be submitted in favor of the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from a Kuwaiti bank, valid for the entire duration of the bid's validity, which is (90) days.
- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage and a valid tax compliance certificate must be submitted.
- A letter of authorization and a copy of the Civil ID of the company representative are required to purchase the tender documents.
- This tender is indivisible, and alternative offers are not permitted.
- The bidder must submit a letter with an attached copy of the registration certificate from the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
- The preliminary meeting is scheduled for Thursday, 10/4/2025, at 11:00 AM.

The bid must remain valid for a period of (90) days from the closing date. The Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> reserves the right to extend or renew this period for any duration it deems appropriate to complete the award procedures.
For inquiries, please call the following numbers:
Direct: 22011412 / 22011438
Email: nt.aldoweesh@da.gov.kw sa.alhasawi@da.gov.kw

Undersecretary for Financial, Administrative, and Personnel Affairs

## Announcement
Regarding Practice No. NCCA – (2) /2025/2026
Maintenance of Security Surveillance Camera Systems and their Accessories for the sites of
the National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters <orig>المجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig>
Specialized companies registered with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> wishing to participate in this practice may obtain the practice documents for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.), only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, from the Financial Affairs Department – Contracts Section – Second Floor – Room (1), National Council building, Al-Shuhada Street – Sharq <orig>الشرق</orig>, within (10 working days) from the date of publication of the announcement in the official gazette, Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>. A preliminary meeting will be held to answer the inquiries of the practitioners on Thursday of the first week of the announcement's publication in the gazette regarding the offering of the practice. The meeting will take place at the main building of the General Secretariat of the National Council <orig>الأمانة العامة للمجلس الوطني</orig> at ten o'clock in the morning. A copy of the practice receipt must be brought.

## Announcement
The National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters <orig>المجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig> announces the offering of Practice No. NCCA – 23 (2024/2025) for an Electronic Correspondence System.
Specialized companies wishing to participate in this practice may obtain the practice documents for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.), only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, from the Financial Affairs Department – Contracts Section – Second Floor – National Council for Culture, Arts, and Letters building, Al-Shuhada Street – Sharq <orig>الشرق</orig>.
Please note that the deadline for submitting bids is within (10 working days from the date of publication of the announcement in the Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> gazette).
All documents must be submitted on three (3) copies of a CD, with the exception of (the bid form, the initial deposit, a copy of the purchase receipt, and the bidder's information form).
*The bid is indivisible, and alternative offers will not be accepted.
*This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend the envelope-opening session, after coordinating with the Procurement Supervision (Contracts Section) before the day scheduled for the bid-opening session.

# Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig>

## Announcement
The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces that Messrs. / Almas International Company for Aluminum Workshops <orig>شركة الماس العالمية لورش الألمنيوم</orig> have applied for the registration of the following in the Industrial Register:
- **License No.:** 209518
- **Activity Type:** Aluminum Works

## Announcement
The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces that Mr. / Abdulwahab Jassim Al-Sumait <orig>عبدالوهاب جاسم الصميط</orig> has applied for the issuance of a replacement for a lost contract for Block No. (1770), Plot 1, in the Al-Rai <orig>الري</orig> area. Anyone who has the aforementioned block contract in their possession or has any information regarding it is requested to come to the headquarters of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> (Ground Floor), Licensing and Industrial Register Department, within two weeks from the date of this announcement. Accordingly, after the expiration of this period, the Authority will issue a replacement for the requested lost contract.

## Announcement
The Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> announces that Al-Hadidiyah Engineering Company for Industries and General Contracting <orig>شركة الحديديبة الهندسية للصناعات والمقاولات العامة</orig> has applied for the issuance of a replacement for a lost contract for Plot No. (38D), Block No. A in the Shuwaikh Industrial Area 2 <orig>منطقة الشويخ الصناعية 2</orig>.
Anyone who is in possession of the aforementioned plot contract or has any information regarding it is requested to come forward to the headquarters of the Public Authority for Industry <orig>الهيئة العامة للصناعة</orig> (Ground Floor), Licensing and Industrial Registry Department, within two weeks from the date of this announcement's publication. Accordingly, after the expiration of this period, the Authority will issue a replacement for the lost contract.

# Capital Markets Authority
## Announcement
The Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> announces the end of the period for Al Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig> to deliver clients' funds and assets to them or to those related to their housing, management, or custody.
The expiration of this period does not exempt Al Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig>, Mr. Saleh Nasser Saleh Al-Saleh <orig>صالح ناصر صالح الصالح</orig>, the company's Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors, or its Board of Directors from any current or future legal liability related to contracts concluded with its clients or related to the process of delivering their funds and assets to them or to those related to their housing, management, or custody, towards the clients of Al Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig> or third parties.
The expiration of the period is not, in any way, to be considered an endorsement by the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> or a validation of the correctness of the process of delivering clients' funds and assets to them or to those related to their housing, management, or custody, nor does it exempt the business dealings of Al Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig> with its clients or with third parties.
Furthermore, the expiration of the period does not constitute a discharge of liability for Al Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig>, Mr. Saleh Nasser Saleh Al-Saleh <orig>صالح ناصر صالح الصالح</orig>, the Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors, its Board of Directors, its executive management, or any person registered in a position or function requiring registration with Al Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig>.

# Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>
Announcement of the Issuance of Practice No. 6/2020/2021(A)
Operation, Management, Training, Monitoring, and Control of Maintenance, Improvements, and Development of Air Navigation Services at Kuwait International Airport
At the request of the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>
The practice documents can be obtained from the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.

<table_caption>Tender Details for Practice No. 6/2020/2021(A)</table_caption>
<table>
| Issuance | Scheduled Bid Submission Date (Closing Date) | Price | Guarantee |
|---|---|---|---|
| 2025/04/06 | 2025/05/04 | 3500 | 450,000 K.D. valid for 90 days in favor of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> |
</table>

Preliminary Meeting (Inquiry Session)
10:00 AM on Monday, 14-04-2025, in the meeting hall of the Planning and Follow-up Department. Site Visit
10:00 AM on Tuesday, 15-04-2025, at the Directorate General of Civil Aviation <orig>الإدارة العامة للطيران المدني</orig>

- The deadline for submitting bids is 1:00 PM on the day specified in the announcement above for bid submission.
- Limited practice in accordance with the provisions of Article (18) of the Public Tenders Law No. (49) of 2016.
- Not divisible
- Alternative offers are not accepted
- The above-mentioned fee is to be paid by a certified check or K-Net card.
- Companies/practitioners wishing to submit inquiries, clarifications, etc., must adhere to submitting them to the concerned entity at the time and place specified in the schedule above for the preliminary meeting (inquiry session). Any inquiries or clarifications submitted to the Agency will not be considered.
- All documents must be submitted on a non-writable CD, except for the bid form and the preliminary guarantee, which must be submitted as hard copies.
- A valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage, issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>, must be submitted with the bid.
- In accordance with the text of Article 48 of the Public Tenders Law No. 49 of 2016, which states:
"Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the tender documents in a public session in the presence of the bidders or their representatives."
The practice documents will be published on the Agency's website for review before proceeding to purchase the documents. In the event the documents are purchased and the prescribed fees are paid, requests for fee refunds will not be accepted except in the case of the practice's cancellation in accordance with the provisions of Article (55) of the Public Tenders Law.
- This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the envelope-opening session.
- Companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Bid Opening Section before the day scheduled for the bid opening session and bring the following documents:
1. A copy of the Civil ID.
2. A copy of the signature authorization specific to the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3. In the event that a person other than the authorized signatory attends, a written letter from the authorized signatory at the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> must be presented, authorizing whomever they deem appropriate to attend the session.
- This announcement is an integral part of the practice documents.
- For more information, please visit our website at WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW
Secretary General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الأمين العام للجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>

| Pre-Bid Meeting (inquiry session) | 2025/4/14 | Planning Department at 9:00 am |
| Site visit | 2025/4/15 | DGCA Planning Department |
</table>

The Tender documents will be published on CAPT website for viewing before purchasing the documents.
When purchasing the documents and payment is fulfilled by the qualified tenderers (listed below), any requests for refund of fees will not be accepted unless the tender is canceled as per Article no. (55) of the Public Tenders Law.
- The final closing time for submitting bids is one o’clock in the afternoon of the day specified in the above announcement, which is scheduled for submitting the bids.
- General Tender in accordance with the provisions of Article No. (18) of Public Tenders Law No. (49) of 2016.
- The tender shall not be divided.
- Alternate offers will not be accepted.
- Payment mentioned above shall be made by either a certified Cheque or K-net card.
- Inquiries or clarifications, etc. from the companies / tenderers – qualified by CAPT (listed below) – to be submitted to the relevant authority at the time and place specified above for the Pre-Bid meeting (inquiry session). Any inquiries or clarifications submitted to the CAPT will not be considered.
- The bid should be presented in two envelopes, Technical and Financial.
- All documents should be submitted on a non-editable CD, except for the bid Price and the initial Bond, which should be submitted as hard copies.
- A valid “National Manpower Percentage Certificate” issued from the Public Authority for Manpower must be submitted – from your local partner – with the bid proposal.
- The ‘Bid envelopes shall be opened at the time and place indicated in the tender documents in a public session in the presence of the bidders or their representatives’ as per the Article no. (48) of the Public Tenders Law No. (49) Year 2016.

# Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>
## Announcement (40/2025)
The holder of the following license has applied to the Municipality:

<table_caption>License Holder Details for Kuwait Municipality Announcement</table_caption>
<table>
| | |
|:---|:---|
| Trade Name | Abdul Hamid Al-Issa General Trading and Contracting Company <orig>شركة عبد الحميد العيسى للتجارة العامة والمقاولات</orig> |
| Category | Building Contractor/Categories |
| Registration Number | 6200027 |
</table>

requesting the release of the company's bank guarantees deposited with the Municipality in exchange for its classification.
Pursuant to Article (19) of Municipality Resolution No. (161/2009) concerning the classification, licensing, and registration of building and demolition contractors in Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>, which stipulates that a contractor may submit a request to the Municipality to cancel their registration before its expiry or to cancel their classification, and the committee stipulated in the first article of these regulations may issue its decision to that effect after fulfilling the following two conditions:
1- The contractor has completed all contracted works.
2- The lapse of (15) fifteen days from the date of publishing this request in the Official Gazette.
The cancellation of the license or registration shall result in the return of the bank guarantee submitted by the contractor, taking into account the last paragraph of Article (10) of this resolution.
Accordingly, the Municipality appeals to anyone who has any claims against the aforementioned contractor regarding building construction contracts concluded between them that have not yet been completed, or judicial attachments in their favor due to violating contracting works or dues arising from the construction contract, to contact the Contractors Section at the Engineering Systems Department within a maximum period of fifteen days from this date. The Municipality will not consider any claims submitted after the specified period.
Director General of the Municipality <orig>مدير عام البلدية</orig>

The General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> announces the issuance of Practice No. (24/2024/2025) for the transportation of employees of the Marine Fire Department from the Salmiya Marine Rescue Center to the Failaka Marine Rescue Center, under the General Fire Force, for a period of two years.

5. A copy of the supplier registration receipt with the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>.
6. The insurance value is 2% of the submitted bid value.
7. A preliminary meeting on Thursday, 17/4/2025.
8. Bids are to be submitted to the Tenders and Contracts Preparation Department at the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> in the Mubarak Al-Abdullah area (West Mishref), first floor.

The deadline for submitting bids is Sunday, 18/5/2025, at 1:00 PM at the Tenders and Contracts Preparation Department in the Mubarak Al-Abdullah area (West Mishref), first floor.

| Issuance Date | Preliminary Meeting Date | Closing Date | Tender Document Purchase Price | Initial Bid Bond Value |
| :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- | :--- |
| Sunday, 6/4/2025 | Monday, 21/4/2025, at 10:00 AM | Tuesday, 13/5/2025, at 1:00 PM | 500/- K.D. (Five hundred Kuwaiti Dinars) | 15,000/- K.D. (Fifteen thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) |
</table>

**Notes:**

*   This is a public tender for specialized companies with pre-qualification conditions. It is indivisible, and alternative bids are not permitted, except where the tender conditions explicitly allow for their submission.
*   No bidder will be allowed to attend the preliminary meeting unless they provide proof of having obtained the tender documents, and if they have not notified Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> of the names and job titles of their nominated attendees at least two days before the preliminary meeting.
*   A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register for classification under more than one name, nor submit more than one bid in a tender. However, a person who has a stake in separate companies, each with its own legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative structure, may register themselves and each of their independent companies for classification. Any bid from a bidder who violates this article shall be considered null and void by rule of law.
*   Any inquiries or requests related to the tender documents must be sent in writing via email no later than 10:00 AM on the day following the preliminary meeting. No requests will be considered for any reason after this deadline.
*   The cost of the tender documents is non-refundable.
*   The initial bid bond must be valid for the entire duration of the bid's validity (90 days from the closing date) and must be submitted in favor of the Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation and its Subsidiaries <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا لمناقصات مؤسسة البترول الكويتية وشركاتها التابعة</orig>.
*   Bids must be addressed with the tender name and number and placed in the designated bid box located at the headquarters of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> – Oil Sector Complex – Shuwaikh – Arabian Gulf Street – (Waiting Room) – next to Gate No. (1) before the specified closing time. Any bid submitted after the specified closing time will be rejected.
*   The bidder must be registered on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation and its subsidiaries (ktendering.com.kw) and must submit a certificate proving this with the bid.
*   Those wishing to participate in the tender are required to send a participation request via email (purch_contracts@kpc.com.kw) with a single PDF file attached, containing the following documents in the order shown:

1.  A letter addressed to Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> from the authorized signatory expressing the desire to participate, including the following company details:
    *   Tender title and number.
    *   Name of the person responsible for coordination between the Corporation and the bidder.
    *   Direct telephone number (mobile + landline).
    *   Email address (for the person + for the company).
    *   Fax number.
    *   Company address.
2.  An official letter from the authorized signatory including the following:
    *   Names of persons authorized to sign on behalf of the company.
    *   Their job titles.
    *   Telephone numbers (mobile + landline).
    *   Email addresses.
3.  A copy of a valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage in non-governmental entities, issued and certified by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>.
4.  A copy of the company's Articles of Association, in addition to the latest amendment contract (if any).
5.  A copy of the commercial license from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
6.  A recent letter (not older than 2022) containing the signature specimen of the person authorized to sign on behalf of the company, certified by the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
7.  A copy of a valid registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
8.  A copy of a valid registration certificate with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
9.  A copy of a valid registration certificate with the Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>.

The meeting link—and other details for joining the meeting—will be sent to all bidders through the commercial electronic platform (K-Tendering portal), which bidders should monitor regularly to stay informed of any

## updates regarding the tender.
- A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register for classification under more than one name, nor submit more than one bid in a tender, with the exception of alternative bids where permitted by the tender conditions.
However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each with its own legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative body, may register themselves and each of their independent companies for classification.
A bid from a bidder who violates this article shall be considered null and void by law, in accordance with Article (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders <orig>القانون رقم (49) لسنة 2016 بشأن المناقصات العامة</orig>.

- The bidder must deposit the fee for purchasing the tender document into the account of the Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> (KW59NBOK00000000002004811204) and submit the receipt with the bid. Bids not accompanied by a payment receipt will be disqualified. If the bid is submitted electronically, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached to the bid electronically.
- Please note that this is a general, non-divisible tender, and supply must be from the factory specified in the tender documents.
- A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register for classification under more than one name, nor submit more than one bid in a tender, with the exception of alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each with its own legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative body, may register themselves and each of their independent companies for classification. A bid from a tenderer who violates this article shall be considered null and void by law, in accordance with Article (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders.

Note:
- All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the commercial electronic platform as specified in the tender documents.
- The Internal Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء الداخلية</orig> would like to draw the attention of bidders who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical specifications to submit such requests a maximum of (two weeks) before the closing date (for this tender). These requests will be rejected and will not be considered for any reason after this deadline.
- To obtain a username and password to access the commercial electronic platform, please call the following phone numbers: 23887794 / 23887792.
cwphelp@knpc.com
- Explanatory instructions on how to submit a bid through the commercial electronic platform are available on our website.

Secretary

The Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig>, a subsidiary of the Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig>, announces its annual plan for all tenders / practices / direct contracts / purchase orders and qualifications expected to be issued during the fiscal year (2025/2026), as per the table below: -

|:---:|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | Providing legal consultancy and business services for Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig> | Legal consultancy and legal services to represent Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig> before the courts of the State of Kuwait and the GCC countries | Two years | First Quarter | Direct Contract | Non-divisible | | Legal consultancy and legal services to represent Kuwait Oil Tanker Company <orig>شركة ناقلات النفط الكويتية</orig> before the courts of the State of Kuwait and the GCC countries |

 2- Evaluating job tasks on a scientific basis to measure risks/hardships using specialized equipment. 3- Identifying the sources and causes of risks and the degree of employee exposure to risks/hardships. 4- Writing a complete job description containing information about the risks/hardships for each job included in this study. 5- Conducting a field survey and measurements that require laboratories to measure risks. ## Announcement
Annual Plan for Supply, Contracting, and Service Contracts

Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces that in accordance with Article (33) and Article (88) of the Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016 regarding the subject of the above-mentioned announcement, the plans are published weekly on the official website of Kuwait Oil Company. Therefore, all those interested in reviewing them should visit the website continuously to obtain the latest updates by following the steps below:
1- The company's website WWW.KOCKW.COM
2- Click on E-business
3- Select one of the options: Tenders (RFPs) or Procurements (RFQs)
4- Click on Upcoming

| 3 | TGS GEOPHYSICAL COMPANY UK LTD |
</table>

- The grievance or request must be submitted at the headquarters of the Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig>, Main Office – Higher Procurement Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation and its Subsidiaries.
- Any party filing a grievance for not being included in the above list, upon submitting a grievance/participation request, must pay a fee of (250/- K.D.) for grievance/participation requests in consideration for studying the possibility of their inclusion in that list. The fee for the grievance/participation request shall be paid via a bank deposit receipt to the Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> account mentioned below:

ACCOUNT NAME: KUWAIT OIL COMPANY

- We would also like to draw the attention of bidders/companies to the fact that, based on the text of Article (29) of Law No. 49 of 2016 regarding Public Tenders, "A single person or a group of persons collectively may not register for classification under more than one name, nor submit more than one bid in a tender, with the exception of alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each with its own legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative body, may register themselves and each of their independent companies for classification. The bid of a tenderer who violates this article shall be considered null and void by law."
- To know the qualification bases and criteria or for any additional information, please visit the unified electronic commercial platform (K–Tendering Portal) on the website of the Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
https://www.ktendering.com.kw →
